<td align="right"><div class="plainlinks hlist navbar mini"><ul><li class="nv-view"><a href="/wiki/Template:%E6%95%B8" title="Template:數"><abbr title="查看该模板">查</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-talk"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:%E6%95%B8" title="Template talk:數"><abbr title="讨论该模板">论</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-edit"><a class="external text" href="https://zh.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:%E6%95%B8&amp;action=edit"><abbr title="编辑该模板">编</abbr></a></li></ul></div>

<p><b>圓周率</b>是一个<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E5%B8%B8%E6%95%B0" title="数学常数">数学常数</a>，为一个<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86" title="圆">圆</a>的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86%E5%91%A8" title="圆周">周长</a>和其<a href="/wiki/%E7%9B%B4%E5%BE%84" title="直径">直径</a>的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AF%94%E7%8E%87" title="比率">比率</a>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%BF%91%E4%BC%BC%E5%80%BC" title="近似值">近似值</a>约等於3.14159265，常用符号<b><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span></b>来表示。
</p><p>因为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是一个<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E7%90%86%E6%95%B0" title="无理数">无理数</a>，所以它不能用<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%88%86%E6%95%B0" title="分数">分数</a>完全表示出来（即它的<a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%8F%E6%95%B0" title="小数">小数</a>部分是一个无限不<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AA%E7%8E%AF%E5%B0%8F%E6%95%B0" title="循环小数">循环小数</a>）。当然，它可以用像<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {22}{7}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>22</mn>
<mn>7</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {22}{7}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\frac {22}{7}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8a48b7aaf32f5f27ba3ffc352f16e3e0ed95680e" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:3.161ex; height:5.343ex;"/></span>般的有理数來近似。<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的数字序列被認為是<a href="/wiki/%E9%9A%8F%E6%9C%BA%E6%95%B0%E5%88%97" title="随机数列">随机分布</a>的，有一种<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E8%A7%84%E6%95%B0" title="正规数">统计上特别的随机性</a>，但至今未能证明。此外，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>还是一个<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B6%85%E8%B6%8A%E6%95%B0" title="超越数">超越数</a>——它不是任何<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E7%90%86%E6%95%B0" title="有理数">有理数</a><a href="/wiki/%E7%B3%BB%E6%95%B0" title="系数">系数</a><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%9A%E9%A1%B9%E5%BC%8F" title="多项式">多项式</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E6%A0%B9_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="根 (数学)">根</a>。由於<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的超越性质，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8C%96%E5%9C%86%E4%B8%BA%E6%96%B9" title="化圆为方">化圆为方</a>的问题不可能用<a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%BA%E8%A7%84%E4%BD%9C%E5%9B%BE" title="尺规作图">尺规作图</a>解决。
</p><p>几个<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%96%87%E6%98%8E%E5%8F%A4%E5%9B%BD" title="文明古国">文明古国</a>在很早就需要计算出<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的较精确的值以便于生产中的计算。公元5世纪时，中國<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8D%97%E6%9C%9D%E5%AE%8B" title="南朝宋">劉宋</a>数学家<a href="/wiki/%E7%A5%96%E5%86%B2%E4%B9%8B" title="祖冲之">祖冲之</a>用几何方法将圆周率计算到小数点后7位数字。大约同一时间，<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%B0%E5%BA%A6" title="印度">印度</a>的数学家也将圆周率计算到小数点后5位。历史上首个<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的精确<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E7%A9%B7%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="无穷级数">无穷级数</a>公式（即<a href="/wiki/%CE%A0%E7%9A%84%E8%8E%B1%E5%B8%83%E5%B0%BC%E8%8C%A8%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="Π的莱布尼茨公式">π的莱布尼茨公式</a>）直到约1000年后才由印度数学家发现。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E7%A9%8D%E5%88%86" title="微積分">微積分</a>的出現，很快地將<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的計算位數推至數百位，足以滿足任何科學工程的計算需求。在20和21世纪，由于<a href="/wiki/%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97%E6%9C%BA%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6" title="计算机科学">计算机技术</a>的快速发展，借助<a class="mw-redirect mw-disambig" href="/wiki/%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97%E6%9C%BA" title="计算机">计算机</a>的计算使得<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的精度急速提高。截至2022年6月，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%81%E8%BF%9B%E5%88%B6" title="十进制">十进制</a>精度已高达1×10<sup>14</sup>位。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup>当前人类计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的值的主要目的是为打破记录、测试<a href="/wiki/%E8%B6%85%E7%BA%A7%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97%E6%9C%BA" title="超级计算机">超级计算机</a>的计算能力和高精度乘法<a href="/wiki/%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95" title="算法">算法</a>，因为几乎所有的科学研究对<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的精度要求都不会超过几百位。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-1"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:17</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup>
</p><p>因为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>在<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%AD%A6" title="三角学">三角学</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E5%87%A0%E4%BD%95%E5%AD%A6" title="几何学">几何学</a>的许多公式，特别是在圆形、椭球形或球形相關公式中广泛应用。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BronshteĭnSemendiaev1971_9-0"><a href="#cite_note-BronshteĭnSemendiaev1971-9">[9]</a></sup>在更近代的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90" title="數學分析">數學分析</a>裡，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>改由<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AF%A6%E6%95%B8" title="實數">實數</a>系統譜性質中的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%E5%80%BC" title="特征值">特征值</a>或<a href="/wiki/%E9%80%B1%E6%9C%9F" title="週期">週期</a>來定義，不再指涉幾何。所以它也在一些和圓之幾何無甚相關的数学和科學領域中出現，像是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E8%AB%96" title="數論">數論</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B5%B1%E8%A8%88" title="統計">統計</a>以及幾乎<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%89%A9%E7%90%86%E5%AD%B8" title="物理學">物理學</a>中的所有領域。<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h2><span id=".E5.9F.BA.E6.9C.AC.E6.A6.82.E5.BF.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="基本概念">基本概念</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：基本概念">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E5.90.8D.E7.A7.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="名称">名称</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：名称">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>数学家用小写<a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%8C%E8%85%8A%E5%AD%97%E6%AF%8D" title="希腊字母">希腊字母</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>表示圆周和其直径之比，有时也将其拼写为“<span lang="en">Pi</span>”，這来自于希腊语“<span lang="el">περίμετρος</span>”（周长）的首字母。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup>在英语中，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的发音与英文单词“Pie”（<span class="nowrap"><span class="IPA nopopups"><a href="/wiki/Help:%E8%8B%B1%E8%AA%9E%E5%9C%8B%E9%9A%9B%E9%9F%B3%E6%A8%99" title="Help:英語國際音標">/<span style="border-bottom:1px dotted"><span title="「pie」的「p」音">p</span><span title="/aɪ/：「tide」的「i」音">aɪ</span></span>/</a></span></span>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A5%BF%E5%BC%8F%E9%A6%85%E9%A5%BC" title="西式馅饼">西式馅饼</a>）相同。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup>在数学中，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的小写字母（或者是其<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E8%A1%AC%E7%BA%BF%E4%BD%93" title="无衬线体">无衬线体</a>）要和表示<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%BF%9E%E4%B9%98%E7%A7%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="连乘积（页面不存在）">连乘积</a>的大写形式Π相区分开。
</p><p>关于為何选择符号<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的原因，请参见<a href="#π符号的引入">π符号的引入</a>一节。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.AE.9A.E4.B9.89"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="定义">定义</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：定义">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Pi_eq_C_over_d_zh.svg"><img alt="A diagram of a circle, with the width labeled as diameter, and the perimeter labeled as circumference" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="512" data-file-width="512" decoding="async" height="220" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Pi_eq_C_over_d_zh.svg/220px-Pi_eq_C_over_d_zh.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Pi_eq_C_over_d_zh.svg/330px-Pi_eq_C_over_d_zh.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Pi_eq_C_over_d_zh.svg/440px-Pi_eq_C_over_d_zh.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Pi_eq_C_over_d_zh.svg" title="放大"></a></div>圆的周长略大于其直径的三倍长。 精确的比例称为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span></div></div></div>
<p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>常用定义为<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86" title="圆">圆</a>的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86%E5%91%A8" title="圆周">周长</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle C}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>C</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle C}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="C" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4fc55753007cd3c18576f7933f6f089196732029" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.766ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>与<a href="/wiki/%E7%9B%B4%E5%BE%84" title="直径">直径</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle d}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>d</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle d}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="d" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e85ff03cbe0c7341af6b982e47e9f90d235c66ab" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.216ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的比值：<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-2"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:8</sup>
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi ={\frac {C}{d}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mi>C</mi>
<mi>d</mi>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi ={\frac {C}{d}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \pi ={\frac {C}{d}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d3ffc6970dda2e60597854f14e2ac1e13a25a5cf" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:7.033ex; height:5.509ex;"/></span>.</dd></dl>
<p>无论圆的大小如何，比值<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {C}{d}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mi>C</mi>
<mi>d</mi>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {C}{d}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {C}{d}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2dd290922de236157985a89833a52a82c9b2350d" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:2.602ex; height:5.509ex;"/></span>为恒值。如果一个圆的直径变为原先的二倍，它的周长也将变为二倍，比值<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {C}{d}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mi>C</mi>
<mi>d</mi>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {C}{d}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {C}{d}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2dd290922de236157985a89833a52a82c9b2350d" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:2.602ex; height:5.509ex;"/></span>不变。当前<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的定义隐性地使用了<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E5%87%A0%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%97%E5%87%A0%E4%BD%95" title="欧几里得几何">欧几里得几何</a>中的一些定理，虽然一个圆的定义可以扩展到任意曲面（即<a href="/wiki/%E9%9D%9E%E6%AC%A7%E5%87%A0%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%97%E5%87%A0%E4%BD%95" title="非欧几里得几何">非欧几里得几何</a>），但这些圆将不再符合定律<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi ={\frac {C}{d}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mi>C</mi>
<mi>d</mi>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi ={\frac {C}{d}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \pi ={\frac {C}{d}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d3ffc6970dda2e60597854f14e2ac1e13a25a5cf" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:7.033ex; height:5.509ex;"/></span>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-3"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup>
</p><p>这里，圆的周长指其圆周的<a href="/wiki/%E5%BC%A7%E9%95%BF" title="弧长">弧长</a>，弧长这一概念可以不依赖几何学，而是使用<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86" title="微积分">微积分</a>学中的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90" title="函数极限">极限</a>来定义。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup>例如，若想计算<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%AC%9B%E5%8D%A1%E5%84%BF%E5%9D%90%E6%A0%87%E7%B3%BB" title="笛卡儿坐标系">笛卡儿坐标系</a>中单位圆<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x^{2}+y^{2}=1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>+</mo>
<msup>
<mi>y</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi =\int _{-1}^{1}{\frac {dx}{\sqrt {1-x^{2}}}}.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>上述积分是由<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8D%A1%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E9%AD%8F%E5%B0%94%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%E6%8B%89%E6%96%AF" title="卡尔·魏尔斯特拉斯">卡尔·魏尔斯特拉斯</a>于1841年对<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mstyle>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的积分定义。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup>
</p><p>这些依赖于周长，且隐性地依赖<a href="/wiki/%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86" title="积分">积分</a>的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的定义，如今在文献中并不常见。雷默特（<a href="#CITEREFRemmert1991">Remmert (1991</a>)）解释说这是因为在现代微积分教学中，大学一般将<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E5%88%86" title="微分">微分学</a>课程安排在积分学课程之前，所以不依赖于后者的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的定义就很有必要了。其中一种定义，由<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Richard Baltzer" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="理查·巴爾策"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%90%86%E6%9F%A5%C2%B7%E5%B7%B4%E7%88%BE%E7%AD%96&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="理查·巴爾策（页面不存在）">理查·巴爾策</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Richard_Baltzer" title="en:Richard Baltzer"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Richard Baltzer</span></a></span>）</span></span>提出，<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup>由<a href="/wiki/%E6%84%9B%E5%BE%B7%E8%92%99%C2%B7%E8%98%AD%E9%81%93" title="愛德蒙·蘭道">愛德蒙·蘭道</a>推广，<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup>其表述如下：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是两倍于能使<a href="/wiki/%E9%A4%98%E5%BC%A6" title="餘弦">余弦函数</a>等于零的最小正数。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-4"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Reinhold_Remmert_1991_129_15-1"><a href="#cite_note-Reinhold_Remmert_1991_129-15">[15]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rudin_1976_19-0"><a href="#cite_note-Rudin_1976-19">[19]</a></sup>余弦函数可以由独立于几何之外的<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%82%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="幂级数">幂级数</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup>定义，或者使用<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E5%88%86%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B" title="微分方程">微分方程</a>的解来定义。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rudin_1976_19-1"><a href="#cite_note-Rudin_1976-19">[19]</a></sup>
</p><p>在相似的启发下，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>并且其中包括一个独特的正实数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>一个基于同样想法，但更为抽象的定义运用了精巧的<a href="/wiki/%E6%8B%93%E6%89%91%E5%AD%A6" title="拓扑学">拓扑学</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6" title="代数学">代数学</a>概念，用以下定理描述：<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup>存在一个唯一的从加法模数整数组成的实数群 <b>R</b>/<b>Z</b> 到绝对值为1的复数组成的乘法群的<a href="/wiki/%E6%80%81%E5%B0%84" title="态射">连续同态</a>（拓扑学概念，指在<a href="/wiki/%E6%8B%93%E6%89%91%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="拓扑空间">拓扑空间</a>之间的一种<a href="/wiki/%E6%80%81%E5%B0%84" title="态射">态射</a>）。数字<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>被定义为此<a href="/wiki/%E5%90%8C%E6%80%81" title="同态">同态</a>派生的模的一半。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Nicolas_Bourbaki_23-0"><a href="#cite_note-Nicolas_Bourbaki-23">[23]</a></sup>
</p><p>在给定的周长的条件下，圆会围成最大的面积，因此<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的表述同樣为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%AD%89%E5%91%A8%E4%B8%8D%E7%AD%89%E5%BC%8F" title="等周不等式">等周不等式</a>中出现的常数（乘四分之一）。此外，在很多其他紧密相关的方程中，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>作为某些几何或者物理过程的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%E5%80%BC" title="特征值">特征值</a>出现；详见<a href="#谱特征">下文</a>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.97.A0.E7.90.86.E6.80.A7.E5.8F.8A.E6.AD.A3.E8.A7.84.E6.80.A7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="无理性及正规性">无理性及正规性</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：无理性及正规性">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是个<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E7%90%86%E6%95%B0" title="无理数">无理数</a>，也就是说，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>无法表示成<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E7%90%86%E6%95%B0" title="有理数">两个整数之比</a>的形式（形如<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {22}{7}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>22</mn>
<mn>7</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {22}{7}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\frac {22}{7}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8a48b7aaf32f5f27ba3ffc352f16e3e0ed95680e" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:3.161ex; height:5.343ex;"/></span>的分数常用来近似表达<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>，但是没有任何<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%86%E6%95%B8" title="分數">普通分数</a>（指整数的比）可以取到<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的精确值）。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-5"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:5</sup>由于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是无理数，故可表示为无限不循环小数。有多种方法能<a href="/wiki/%E8%AF%81%E6%98%8E%CF%80%E6%98%AF%E6%97%A0%E7%90%86%E6%95%B0" title="证明π是无理数">证明π是无理数</a>，这些证明也都要用到<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AD%A6" title="微积分学">微积分学</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8D%E8%AF%81%E6%B3%95" title="反证法">反证法</a>。人们還無法準確得知<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>可以用<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E7%90%86%E6%95%B0" title="有理数">有理数</a>来近似的程度（稱為<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%84%A1%E7%90%86%E6%80%A7%E5%BA%A6%E9%87%8F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="無理性度量（页面不存在）">無理性度量</a>），不過估計其無理性度量比<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml"><i>e</i></span></span>或<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml">ln(2)</span></span>的要大，但是小於<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%98%E7%BB%B4%E5%B0%94%E6%95%B0" title="刘维尔数">刘维尔数</a>的無理性度量<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup>。
</p><p>人们通過<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="statistical randomness" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="統計隨機性"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%B5%B1%E8%A8%88%E9%9A%A8%E6%A9%9F%E6%80%A7&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="統計隨機性（页面不存在）">統計隨機性</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/statistical_randomness" title="en:statistical randomness"><span dir="auto" lang="en">statistical randomness</span></a></span>）</span></span>检验，包括<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E8%A7%84%E6%95%B0" title="正规数">正规数</a>的检验，验证了<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的位數沒有明顯的固定模式。因此，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的小数中任意固定长度的序列（例如3位數字的000,001……999）出現機率都相同<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-random_25-0"><a href="#cite_note-random-25">[25]</a></sup>。不過有關<span class="texhtml">π</span>是<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E8%A7%84%E6%95%B0" title="正规数">正规数</a>的猜想既無證明，亦無<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%AF%81%E4%BC%AA" title="证伪">证伪</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-6"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:22-23</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-random_25-1"><a href="#cite_note-random-25">[25]</a></sup>。
</p><p>電腦的出現使得人们可以生成大量<span class="texhtml">π</span>的不同位数，并進行統計分析。<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%91%E7%94%B0%E5%BA%B7%E6%AD%A3" title="金田康正">金田康正</a>針對<span class="texhtml">π</span>的十進制數字進行了詳細的統計分析，并验证了其分布的正规性：例如，將出現0到9十個數字的頻率進行<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%81%87%E8%A8%AD%E6%AA%A2%E5%AE%9A" title="假設檢定">假設檢定</a>，找不到有特定重复规律的證據<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-7"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:22, 28–30</sup>。根據<a href="/wiki/%E7%84%A1%E9%99%90%E7%8C%B4%E5%AD%90%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="無限猴子定理">無限猴子定理</a>，任何任意長度，由隨機內容組成的子序列都有可能看起來像不隨機产生的。因此，就算<span class="texhtml">π</span>的小数序列通過了隨機性統計測試，其中也可能有幾位的數字看起來似有规律可循而非隨機数，例如<span class="texhtml">π</span>的十進制写法中，自第762位小數后开始出现了<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%80%A3%E7%BA%8C%E5%85%AD%E5%80%8B%E7%9A%849" title="連續六個的9">連續六個的9</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-8"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:3</sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.B6.85.E8.B6.8A.E6.80.A7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="超越性">超越性</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：超越性">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Squaring_the_circle.svg"><img alt="A diagram of a square and circle, both with identical area; the length of the side of the square is the square root of pi" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="281" data-file-width="281" decoding="async" height="220" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Squaring_the_circle.svg/220px-Squaring_the_circle.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Squaring_the_circle.svg/330px-Squaring_the_circle.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Squaring_the_circle.svg/440px-Squaring_the_circle.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Squaring_the_circle.svg" title="放大"></a></div>由于<span class="texhtml">π</span>是<a href="/wiki/%E8%B6%85%E8%B6%8A%E6%95%B8" title="超越數">超越數</a>，不能利用<a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%BA%E8%A7%84%E4%BD%9C%E5%9B%BE" title="尺规作图">尺规作图</a><a href="/wiki/%E5%8C%96%E5%9C%93%E7%82%BA%E6%96%B9" title="化圓為方">化圓為方</a>。</div></div></div>
<p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>不仅是个无理数，还是一个<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B6%85%E8%B6%8A%E6%95%B0" title="超越数">超越数</a>，即<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>不是任何一个有理数系数<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%9A%E9%A1%B9%E5%BC%8F" title="多项式">多项式</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E6%A0%B9_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="根 (数学)">根</a>。（比方说，试图通过解有限项方程<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {x^{5}}{120}}-{\frac {x^{3}}{6}}+x=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mrow>
</msup>
<mn>6</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {x^{5}}{120}}-{\frac {x^{3}}{6}}+x=0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {x^{5}}{120}}-{\frac {x^{3}}{6}}+x=0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3bd89ac9c62c9b81bb1f557f0f6ab4894a4db389" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:18.815ex; height:5.676ex;"/></span>，来求得<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的值。）<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ttop_26-0"><a href="#cite_note-ttop-26">[26]</a></sup><span id="noteTag-cite_ref-sup"><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[註 1]</a></sup></span>
</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的超越性衍生出了一些重要的结果：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>不能通过有理数经有限次四则运算和开平方运算来获得，因此<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>不是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A7%84%E7%9F%A9%E6%95%B0" title="规矩数">规矩数</a>。换言之，利用<a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%BA%E8%A7%84%E4%BD%9C%E5%9B%BE" title="尺规作图">尺规作图</a>作不出长度为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的线段，也就不可能用尺规方法做出一个与已知圆面积相等的正方形。后者即为有名的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8C%96%E5%9C%93%E7%82%BA%E6%96%B9" title="化圓為方">化圓為方</a>问题，该问题早在<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%85%B8%E6%97%B6%E4%BB%A3" title="古典时代">古典时代</a>即已提出，曾困扰人们数千年之久<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28">[27]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29">[28]</a></sup>。直至今天，依然有<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B0%91%E7%A7%91" title="民科">民间数学爱好者</a>声称他们解决了这一问题<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30">[29]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.BF.9E.E5.88.86.E5.BC.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="连分式">连分式</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：连分式">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>像所有的无理数一样，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>无法表示成一个<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%88%86%E6%95%B0" title="分数">分数</a>。但是每一个无理数，包括<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>，都能表示成一系列叫做<a href="/wiki/%E8%BF%9E%E5%88%86%E6%95%B0" title="连分数">连分数</a>的连续分数形式：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi =3+\textstyle {\frac {1}{7+\textstyle {\frac {1}{15+\textstyle {\frac {1}{1+\textstyle {\frac {1}{292+\textstyle {\frac {1}{1+\textstyle {\frac {1}{1+\textstyle {\frac {1}{1+\ddots }}}}}}}}}}}}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>在这个连分数的任意一点截断化简，都能得到一个<span class="texhtml">π</span>的近似值；前四个近似值是：3，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {22}{7}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</semantics>

</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>最广为人知且广為使用的几个近似值。用以上方式得出的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的近似值要比任何有相同或更小的整数分母的其他整数分数近似值更接近<span class="texhtml">π</span>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Eymard_1999_78_31-0"><a href="#cite_note-Eymard_1999_78-31">[30]</a></sup>由于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是一个超越数，据超越数定义来说它不是<a href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8%E6%95%B8" title="代數數">代數數</a>，又因此不可能是一个<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%8C%E6%AC%A1%E7%84%A1%E7%90%86%E6%95%B8" title="二次無理數">二次無理數</a>；是故<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>不能表示为<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AA%E7%92%B0%E9%80%A3%E5%88%86%E6%95%B8" title="循環連分數">循环连分数</a>。尽管<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的简单连分数没有表现出任何其他明显规律，<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_32-0"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-32">[31]</a></sup>数学家们發現了数个广义连分数能表示<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>，例如：<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33">[32]</a></sup>
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi =\textstyle {\cfrac {4}{1+\textstyle {\frac {1^{2}}{2+\textstyle {\frac {3^{2}}{2+\textstyle {\frac {5^{2}}{2+\textstyle {\frac {7^{2}}{2+\textstyle {\frac {9^{2}}{2+\ddots }}}}}}}}}}}}=3+\textstyle {\frac {1^{2}}{6+\textstyle {\frac {3^{2}}{6+\textstyle {\frac {5^{2}}{6+\textstyle {\frac {7^{2}}{6+\textstyle {\frac {9^{2}}{6+\ddots }}}}}}}}}}=\textstyle {\cfrac {4}{1+\textstyle {\frac {1^{2}}{3+\textstyle {\frac {2^{2}}{5+\textstyle {\frac {3^{2}}{7+\textstyle {\frac {4^{2}}{9+\ddots }}}}}}}}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".E8.BF.91.E4.BC.BC.E5.80.BC"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="近似值">近似值</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：近似值">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87%E8%BF%91%E4%BC%BC%E5%80%BC" title="圆周率近似值">圆周率近似值</a>包括：
</p>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B4%E6%95%B0" title="整数">整数</a></b>：<a href="/wiki/3" title="3">3</a></li>
<li><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%88%86%E6%95%B0" title="分数">分数</a></b>（依准确度顺序排列）：<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r72900767">.mw-parser-output .sfrac{white-space:nowrap}.mw-parser-output .sfrac.tion,.mw-parser-output .sfrac .tion{display:inline-block;vertical-align:-0.5em;font-size:85%;text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .sfrac .num,.mw-parser-output .sfrac .den{display:block;line-height:1em;margin:0 0.1em}.mw-parser-output .sfrac .den{border-top:1px solid}.mw-parser-output .sr-only{border:0;clip:rect(0,0,0,0);height:1px;margin:-1px;overflow:hidden;padding:0;position:absolute;width:1px}</style><span class="sfrac tion" role="math"><span class="num">22</span><span class="sr-only">/</span><span class="den">7</span></span>、<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r72900767" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="sfrac tion" role="math"><span class="num">333</span><span class="sr-only">/</span><span class="den">106</span></span>、<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r72900767" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="sfrac tion" role="math"><span class="num">355</span><span class="sr-only">/</span><span class="den">113</span></span>、<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r72900767" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="sfrac tion" role="math"><span class="num">52163</span><span class="sr-only">/</span><span class="den">16604</span></span>、<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r72900767" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="sfrac tion" role="math"><span class="num">103993</span><span class="sr-only">/</span><span class="den">33102</span></span>、<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r72900767" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="sfrac tion" role="math"><span class="num">245850922</span><span class="sr-only">/</span><span class="den">78256779</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Eymard_1999_78_31-1"><a href="#cite_note-Eymard_1999_78-31">[30]</a></sup>（选自 <a class="external text" href="//oeis.org/A063674" rel="nofollow">A063674</a> 及 <a class="external text" href="//oeis.org/A063673" rel="nofollow">A063673</a>。）</li>
<li><b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B0%8F%E6%95%B8" title="小數">小數</a></b>（整数后首80个位）：<span style="white-space: nowrap">3.14159<span style="margin-left: 0.25em">26535</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">89793</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">23846</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">26433</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">83279</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">50288</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">41971</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">69399</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">37510</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">58209</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">74944</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">59230</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">78164</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">06286</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">20899...</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-9"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:240</sup>（另见 <a class="external text" href="//oeis.org/A000796" rel="nofollow">A000796</a>）</li></ul>
<p><b>其他进位制中的近似值</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%8C%E8%BF%9B%E5%88%B6" title="二进制">二进制</a>（整数后首48个位）：<span style="white-space: nowrap">11.0010<span style="margin-left: 0.25em">0100</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">0011</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">1111</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">0110</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">1010</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">1000</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">1000</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">1000</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">0101</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">1010</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">0011…</span></span></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E8%BF%9B%E5%88%B6" title="十六进制">十六进制</a>（整数后首20个位）：<span style="white-space: nowrap">3.243F<span style="margin-left: 0.25em">6A88</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">85A3</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">08D3</span><span style="margin-left: 0.25em">1319…</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-10"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:242</sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%AD%E5%8D%81%E9%80%B2%E4%BD%8D" title="六十進位">六十进制</a>（整数后首20个位）：3;8,29,44,0,47,25,53,7,24,57,36,17,43,4,29,7,10,3,41,17…<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-base_60_3-1"><a href="#cite_note-base_60-3">[3]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-base_60_OEIS_4-1"><a href="#cite_note-base_60_OEIS-4">[4]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span id=".E5.A4.8D.E6.95.B0.E4.B8.8E.E6.AC.A7.E6.8B.89.E6.81.92.E7.AD.89.E5.BC.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="复数与欧拉恒等式">复数与欧拉恒等式</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：复数与欧拉恒等式">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Euler%27s_formula.svg"><img alt="在复平面上以原点为圆心的单位圆内，一条射线从圆心出发至圆的边上，以此射线与圆的边的交点作与x轴的垂线并标注了夹角φ和sinφ、cosφ函数" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="549" data-file-width="512" decoding="async" height="236" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Euler%27s_formula.svg/220px-Euler%27s_formula.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Euler%27s_formula.svg/330px-Euler%27s_formula.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Euler%27s_formula.svg/440px-Euler%27s_formula.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Euler%27s_formula.svg" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="欧拉公式">欧拉公式</a>给出了<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml"><i>e</i></span></span>的复指数与<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%8D%E5%B9%B3%E9%9D%A2" title="复平面">复平面</a>上以<a href="/wiki/%E5%8E%9F%E9%BB%9E" title="原點">原點</a>为圆心的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E5%9C%86" title="单位圆">单位圆</a>上的<a href="/wiki/%E7%82%B9" title="点">点</a>之间的关系。</div></div></div>
<p>任何<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="复数 (数学)">复数</a>（以<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle z}</annotation>

</math></span><img alt="z" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bf368e72c009decd9b6686ee84a375632e11de98" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.088ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>为例）都可以表示为一组<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0" title="实数">实数</a>对：在<a href="/wiki/%E6%9E%81%E5%9D%90%E6%A0%87%E7%B3%BB" title="极坐标系">极坐标系</a>中，一个实数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle r}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%8D%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90" title="复分析">复分析</a>中，<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="欧拉公式">欧拉公式</a>将<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="三角函数">三角函数</a>与复<a href="/wiki/%E6%8C%87%E6%95%B0%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="指数函数">指数函数</a>糅合在一起<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EF_35-0"><a href="#cite_note-EF-35">[34]</a></sup>：
</p>

<p>欧拉公式确立了<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="e" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cd253103f0876afc68ebead27a5aa9867d927467" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.083ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的复指数与复平面上以原点为圆心的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E5%9C%86" title="单位圆">单位圆</a>上的点之间的关系，而且当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \varphi =\pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>φ<!-- φ --></mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \varphi =\pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \varphi =\pi }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3f181a336ae10f53a432232ff83696fbdeb4e622" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.951ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>时，欧拉公式就能改写为<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%90%E6%8B%89%E6%81%86%E7%AD%89%E5%BC%8F" title="歐拉恆等式">歐拉恆等式</a>的形式：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {{{e}^{{i}\,{\pi }}}+{1}}=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".E8.B0.B1.E7.89.B9.E5.BE.81"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="谱特征">谱特征</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：谱特征">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Harmonic_partials_on_strings.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="590" data-file-width="620" decoding="async" height="209" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/Harmonic_partials_on_strings.svg/220px-Harmonic_partials_on_strings.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/Harmonic_partials_on_strings.svg/330px-Harmonic_partials_on_strings.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/Harmonic_partials_on_strings.svg/440px-Harmonic_partials_on_strings.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Harmonic_partials_on_strings.svg" title="放大"></a></div>震盪弦的<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%9B%E9%9F%B3" title="泛音">泛音</a>是二次微分的<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%AC%E5%BE%B5%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="本徵函數">本徵函數</a>，會形成<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%9B%E9%9F%B3%E5%88%97" title="泛音列">泛音列</a>。對應的本徵值會形成由<span class="texhtml">π</span>整數倍組成的<a href="/wiki/%E7%AD%89%E5%B7%AE%E6%95%B0%E5%88%97" title="等差数列">等差数列</a></div></div></div>
<p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>经常<a href="#用途">出现</a>在和几何相关的问题之中。然而，在不少和几何无关的问题中也可以看到<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>

</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>

</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \lambda =\pi }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3edde53516da0410b6f5a99e15a18a07cec654c4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.786ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38"><a href="#cite_note-38">[37]</a></sup>。
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sir_William_Thompson_illustration_of_Carthage.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="287" data-file-width="286" decoding="async" height="221" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/Sir_William_Thompson_illustration_of_Carthage.png/220px-Sir_William_Thompson_illustration_of_Carthage.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/d/d8/Sir_William_Thompson_illustration_of_Carthage.png 1.5x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sir_William_Thompson_illustration_of_Carthage.png" title="放大"></a></div>依照<a href="/wiki/%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%80%E4%BB%A3%E5%BC%80%E5%B0%94%E6%96%87%E7%94%B7%E7%88%B5%E5%A8%81%E5%BB%89%C2%B7%E6%B1%A4%E5%A7%86%E6%A3%AE" title="第一代开尔文男爵威廉·汤姆森">第一代开尔文男爵威廉·汤姆森</a>所述的一個傳說，<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E8%BF%A6%E5%A4%AA%E5%9F%BA" title="古迦太基">古迦太基</a>城的外形是等周長問題的一個解（<a href="#CITEREFThompson1894">Thompson 1894</a>）。這些包圍著海的區域是迦太基女王<a href="/wiki/%E7%8B%84%E5%A4%9A" title="狄多">狄多</a>所圍的，城不靠海的邊界需要用一塊指定大小的牛皮圍住，後來是將牛皮剪成小段</div></div></div>
<p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>此例中等號成立的條件恰好是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>等號成立的條件是曲线為一圓形，因為<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A=\pi r^{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>圓周率<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是一維及二維的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Dirichlet energy" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="狄氏能量"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%8B%84%E6%B0%8F%E8%83%BD%E9%87%8F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="狄氏能量（页面不存在）">狄氏能量</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dirichlet_energy" title="en:Dirichlet energy"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Dirichlet energy</span></a></span>）</span></span><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%E5%90%91%E9%87%8F" title="特征向量">特征向量</a>最佳值中，最小的一個，因此<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>會出現在許多經典的物理現象中，例如經典的<a href="/wiki/%E4%BD%8D%E5%8A%BF%E8%AE%BA" title="位势论">位势论</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42"><a href="#cite_note-42">[41]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43"><a href="#cite_note-43">[42]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44"><a href="#cite_note-44">[43]</a></sup>。其一維的情形即為維廷格不等式。
</p><p>圓周率<span class="texhtml">π</span>也是<a href="/wiki/%E5%82%85%E9%87%8C%E5%8F%B6%E5%8F%98%E6%8D%A2" title="傅里叶变换">傅里叶变换</a>的一個重要常數，傅里叶变换屬於<a href="/wiki/%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%8F%98%E6%8D%A2" title="积分变换">积分变换</a>，將一個在實數線上的一個有複數值，可積分的函數，轉換為以下的型式：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\hat {f}}(\xi )=\int _{-\infty }^{\infty }f(x)e^{-2\pi ix\xi }\,dx.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
