</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%8D%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E6%80%A7%E5%8E%9F%E7%90%86" title="不确定性原理">不确定性原理</a>中也有出現<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>物理的結果，有關<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%8F%E5%AD%90%E5%8A%9B%E5%AD%A6" title="量子力学">量子力学</a>中同時觀測位置及動量的不確定性，<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87#描述物理现象" title="圓周率">見下文</a>。傅立葉分析中<span class="texhtml">π</span>的出現是<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Stone–von Neumann theorem" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="史東–馮紐曼定理"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8F%B2%E6%9D%B1%E2%80%93%E9%A6%AE%E7%B4%90%E6%9B%BC%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="史東–馮紐曼定理（页面不存在）">史東–馮紐曼定理</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stone%E2%80%93von_Neumann_theorem" title="en:Stone–von Neumann theorem"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Stone–von Neumann theorem</span></a></span>）</span></span>的結果，證實了<a href="/wiki/%E6%B5%B7%E6%A3%AE%E4%BC%AF%E7%BE%A4" title="海森伯群">海森伯群</a>的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Schrödinger representation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="薛定諤表示"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%96%9B%E5%AE%9A%E8%AB%A4%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="薛定諤表示（页面不存在）">薛定諤表示</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Schr%C3%B6dinger_representation" title="en:Schrödinger representation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Schrödinger representation</span></a></span>）</span></span>的唯一性<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46"><a href="#cite_note-46">[45]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E9.AB.98.E6.96.AF.E7.A7.AF.E5.88.86"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="高斯积分">高斯积分</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：高斯积分">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:E%5E(-x%5E2).svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="600" decoding="async" height="176" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/E%5E%28-x%5E2%29.svg/220px-E%5E%28-x%5E2%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/E%5E%28-x%5E2%29.svg/330px-E%5E%28-x%5E2%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/E%5E%28-x%5E2%29.svg/440px-E%5E%28-x%5E2%29.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:E%5E(-x%5E2).svg" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="高斯函数">高斯函数</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)=e^{-x^{2}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p><a href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86" title="高斯积分">高斯积分</a>是对<a href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="高斯函数">高斯函数</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e^{-x^{2}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Random_walk_simulation.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="662" data-file-width="1070" decoding="async" height="136" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Random_walk_simulation.png/220px-Random_walk_simulation.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Random_walk_simulation.png/330px-Random_walk_simulation.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Random_walk_simulation.png/440px-Random_walk_simulation.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Random_walk_simulation.png" title="放大"></a></div>由一维<a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%83%E6%9C%97%E8%BF%90%E5%8A%A8" title="布朗运动">布朗运动</a>的反正弦定律，可以通过试验正信号相对于负信号领先权过零点的分布反过来推算<span class="texhtml">π</span></div></div></div>
<p>概率论与统计学中的<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E5%BF%83%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="中心极限定理">中心极限定理</a>解释了正态分布以及<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的核心作用，这个定理本质上是联系着<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的<a href="#谱特征">谱特征</a>与<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B5%B7%E6%A3%AE%E5%A0%A1" title="海森堡">海森堡</a><a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%8D%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E6%80%A7%E5%8E%9F%E7%90%86" title="不确定性原理">不确定性原理</a>相关的特征值，并且在不确定性原理中有
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sigma _{x}\sigma _{p}\geq \hbar /2}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>这里的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sigma _{x}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>同样地，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.8E.86.E5.8F.B2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="历史">历史</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：历史">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87%E8%BF%91%E4%BC%BC%E5%80%BC" title="圆周率近似值">π的近似值</a></div>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">参见：<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87%E8%A8%88%E7%AE%97%E5%B9%B4%E8%A1%A8" title="圓周率計算年表">π計算年表</a></div>
<h3><span id=".E8.BF.9C.E5.8F.A4.E6.97.B6.E6.9C.9F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="远古时期">远古时期</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="编辑章节：远古时期">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>圓周率在远古时期（<a href="/wiki/%E5%89%8D1%E5%8D%83%E7%BA%AA" title="前1千纪">公元前一千纪</a>）已估算至前两位（“3”和“1”）。有些<a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%83%E5%8F%8A%E5%AD%A6" title="埃及学">埃及學家</a>聲稱，遠至<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E7%8E%8B%E5%9C%8B%E6%99%82%E6%9C%9F" title="古王國時期">古王國時期</a>時期的古埃及人已經用<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {22}{7}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>22</mn>
<mn>7</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {22}{7}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\frac {22}{7}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8a48b7aaf32f5f27ba3ffc352f16e3e0ed95680e" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:3.161ex; height:5.343ex;"/></span>作為圓周率的約數<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51"><a href="#cite_note-51">[50]</a></sup><span id="noteTag-cite_ref-sup"><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53"><a href="#cite_note-53">[註 2]</a></sup></span>，但這個說法受到了質疑。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rossi_54-0"><a href="#cite_note-Rossi-54">[52]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55"><a href="#cite_note-55">[53]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56"><a href="#cite_note-56">[54]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57"><a href="#cite_note-57">[55]</a></sup>
</p><p>最早有記載的对圓周率估值在<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%9F%83%E5%8F%8A" title="古埃及">古埃及</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B4%E6%AF%94%E4%BC%A6" title="巴比伦">巴比伦</a>出现，兩個估值都与圆周率的正确数值相差不到百分之一。巴比伦曾出土一塊公元前1900至1600年的<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%A5%E6%9D%BF" title="泥板">泥板</a>，泥板上的幾何學陳述暗示了人们当时把圓周率視同<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {25}{8}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>25</mn>
<mn>8</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {25}{8}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {25}{8}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5374f1d2966a9af3579f84900a272b125302ba03" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:3.161ex; height:5.176ex;"/></span>（等於3.125）。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-11"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:167</sup>埃及的<a href="/wiki/%E8%8E%B1%E5%9B%A0%E5%BE%B7%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E7%BA%B8%E8%8D%89%E4%B9%A6" title="莱因德数学纸草书">莱因德数学纸草书</a>（鉴定撰寫年份為公元前1650年，但抄自一份公元前1850年的文本）載有用作計算圓面積的公式，该公式中圓周率等于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle ({\frac {16}{9}})^{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>16</mn>
<mn>9</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
<msup>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>

</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle ({\frac {16}{9}})^{2}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle ({\frac {16}{9}})^{2}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5b26b5e564918a8c05641b6ea594836e80f109cf" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:6.025ex; height:5.176ex;"/></span>（約等於3.1605）。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-12"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:167</sup>
</p><p>公元前4世紀的《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Shatapatha Brahmana" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="百道梵書"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%99%BE%E9%81%93%E6%A2%B5%E6%9B%B8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="百道梵書（页面不存在）">百道梵書</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shatapatha_Brahmana" title="en:Shatapatha Brahmana"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Shatapatha Brahmana</span></a></span>）</span></span>》中的天文學運算把<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {339}{108}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.89.B2.E5.9C.86.E6.97.B6.E4.BB.A3"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="割圆时代">割圆时代</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="编辑章节：割圆时代">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:352px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Archimedes_pi.svg"><img alt="圖中有圓的外切五邊形、內接五邊形、外切六邊形及內接六邊形" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="250" data-file-width="750" decoding="async" height="117" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c9/Archimedes_pi.svg/350px-Archimedes_pi.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c9/Archimedes_pi.svg/525px-Archimedes_pi.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c9/Archimedes_pi.svg/700px-Archimedes_pi.svg.png 2x" width="350"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Archimedes_pi.svg" title="放大"></a></div><span class="texhtml">π</span>可以透過計算圓的外切多邊形及內接多邊形周長來估算</div></div></div>
<p>第一個有紀錄、嚴謹計算<span class="texhtml">π</span>數值的演算法是透過正多邊形的幾何算法，是在西元前250年由希臘數學家<a href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E5%9F%BA%E7%B1%B3%E5%BE%B7" title="阿基米德">阿基米德</a>所發明。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-14"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:170</sup>這個算法使用了有一千年之久，因而有時<span class="texhtml">π</span>亦稱阿基米德常數。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-15"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:175、205</sup>阿基米德的算法是在計算圓的外切正六邊形及內接正六邊形的邊長，以此計算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的上限及下限，之後再將六邊形變成十二邊形，繼續計算邊長……，一直計算到正96邊形為止。他根據多邊形的邊長證明<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {223}{71}}&lt;\pi &lt;{\frac {22}{7}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Archimedes_by_Giuseppe_Nogari.png"><img alt="獨自研究圖形的阿基米德" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="962" data-file-width="798" decoding="async" height="205" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Archimedes_by_Giuseppe_Nogari.png/170px-Archimedes_by_Giuseppe_Nogari.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Archimedes_by_Giuseppe_Nogari.png/255px-Archimedes_by_Giuseppe_Nogari.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Archimedes_by_Giuseppe_Nogari.png/340px-Archimedes_by_Giuseppe_Nogari.png 2x" width="170"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Archimedes_by_Giuseppe_Nogari.png" title="放大"></a></div>阿基米德發展了用多邊形近似<span class="texhtml">π</span>的計算方式</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E5%9B%BD%E5%8E%86%E5%8F%B2" title="中国历史">中国历史</a>上，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {142}{45}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e15c1a1a83a086cc3a659cebaf7b546fed140d55" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:4.323ex; height:5.343ex;"/></span>（第三世紀，數值約3.1556）<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-18"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:176–177</sup>。大約在公元265年，<a href="/wiki/%E6%9B%B9%E9%AD%8F" title="曹魏">曹魏</a>的數學家<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%98%E5%BE%BD" title="刘徽">刘徽</a>創立了<a href="/wiki/%E5%89%B2%E5%9C%86%E6%9C%AF_(%E5%88%98%E5%BE%BD)" title="割圆术 (刘徽)">割圆术</a>，用3,072邊的正多邊形計算出<span class="texhtml">π</span>的數值為3.1416。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated202_63-0"><a href="#cite_note-autogenerated202-63">[61]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-19"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:177</sup>刘徽後來又發明了一個較快的算法，利用邊數差兩倍的正多邊形，其面積的差值會形成等比數列，其公比為<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {1}{4}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>1</mn>
<mn>4</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {1}{4}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\frac{1}{4}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a2dfb63ee75ec084f2abb25d248bc151a2687508" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:1.999ex; height:5.176ex;"/></span>的原理，配合96邊形算出<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的值在3.1415926和3.1415927之间。他同时提出了<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的约率22/7和密率355/113。在之後的八百年內，這都是準確度最高的<span class="texhtml">π</span>估計值。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-20"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:178</sup>為紀念<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A5%96%E6%B2%96%E4%B9%8B" title="祖沖之">祖沖之</a>對圓周率發展的貢獻，<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A5%E6%9C%AC" title="日本">日本</a>數學家<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%89%E4%B8%8A%E7%BE%A9%E5%A4%AB" title="三上義夫">三上義夫</a>將這一推算值命名為“祖沖之圓周率”，簡稱“祖率”。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64"><a href="#cite_note-64">[62]</a></sup>
</p><p>印度天文學家<a href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E8%80%B6%E6%B3%A2%E5%A4%9A" title="阿耶波多">阿耶波多</a>在公元499年的著作《<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E9%87%8C%E4%BA%9A%E5%93%88%E5%A1%94%E5%8E%86%E4%B9%A6" title="阿里亚哈塔历书">阿里亞哈塔曆書</a>》中使用了3.1416的數值。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-21"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:179</sup><a href="/wiki/%E6%96%90%E6%B3%A2%E9%82%A3%E5%A5%91" title="斐波那契">斐波那契</a>在大約1220年利用獨立於阿基米德多邊形法，計算出3.1418<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-22"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:180</sup>。義大利作家<a href="/wiki/%E4%BD%86%E4%B8%81%C2%B7%E9%98%BF%E5%88%A9%E5%90%89%E8%80%B6%E9%87%8C" title="但丁·阿利吉耶里">但丁·阿利吉耶里</a>用的數值則是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 3+{\frac {\sqrt {2}}{10}}\approx 3.14142}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>+</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<msqrt>
<mn>2</mn>
</msqrt>
<mn>10</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
<mo>≈<!-- ≈ --></mo>
<mn>3.14142</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 3+{\frac {\sqrt {2}}{10}}\approx 3.14142}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 3+{\frac {\sqrt {2}}{10}}\approx 3.14142}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/505012ce076df79110687fbea921b3b3b917d7ed" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:18.657ex; height:5.843ex;"/></span>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-23"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:180</sup>
</p><p>波斯天文學家<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%A1%E8%A5%BF" title="卡西">卡西</a>在1424年利用3×2<sup>28</sup>邊的多邊形，計算到六十進制的第9位小數，相當十進制的第16位小數。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65"><a href="#cite_note-65">[63]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66"><a href="#cite_note-66">[64]</a></sup>這一突破成為當時的紀錄，延續了約180年。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_f_67-0"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt_f-67">[65]</a></sup>法國數學家<a href="/wiki/%E5%BC%97%E6%9C%97%E7%B4%A2%E7%93%A6%C2%B7%E9%9F%A6%E8%BE%BE" title="弗朗索瓦·韦达">弗朗索瓦·韦达</a>在1579年用3×2<sup>17</sup>邊形計算到第9位小數<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_f_67-1"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt_f-67">[65]</a></sup>，佛蘭芒數學家<a href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E5%BE%B7%E9%87%8C%E5%AE%89%C2%B7%E8%8C%83%C2%B7%E7%BE%85%E9%96%80" title="阿德里安·范·羅門">阿德里安·范·羅門</a>在1593年計算到第15位小數<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_f_67-2"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt_f-67">[65]</a></sup>。荷蘭數學家<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%B2%81%E9%81%93%E5%A4%AB%C2%B7%E8%8C%83%C2%B7%E7%A7%91%E4%BC%8A%E4%BC%A6" title="鲁道夫·范·科伊伦">鲁道夫·范·科伊伦</a>在1596年計算到第20位小數，他之後又計算到第35位小數（因此在二十世紀初之前，圓周率在德國會稱為鲁道夫數）。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-24"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:182–183</sup>荷蘭科學家<a href="/wiki/%E5%A8%81%E7%90%86%E5%8D%9A%C2%B7%E5%8F%B8%E4%B9%83%E8%80%B3" title="威理博·司乃耳">威理博·司乃耳</a>在1621年計算到第34位小數<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-25"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:183</sup>，而奧地利天文學家<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Christoph Grienberger" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="克里斯托夫·格林伯格"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%85%8B%E9%87%8C%E6%96%AF%E6%89%98%E5%A4%AB%C2%B7%E6%A0%BC%E6%9E%97%E4%BC%AF%E6%A0%BC&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="克里斯托夫·格林伯格（页面不存在）">克里斯托夫·格林伯格</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christoph_Grienberger" title="en:Christoph Grienberger"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Christoph Grienberger</span></a></span>）</span></span>在1630年用10<sup>40</sup>邊形計算到第38位小數<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68"><a href="#cite_note-68">[66]</a></sup>，至今這仍是利用多邊形算法可以達到最準確的結果<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-26"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:183</sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.97.A0.E7.A9.B7.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="无穷级数">无穷级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="编辑章节：无穷级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Comparison_pi_infinite_series.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="256" data-file-width="512" decoding="async" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Comparison_pi_infinite_series.svg/300px-Comparison_pi_infinite_series.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Comparison_pi_infinite_series.svg/450px-Comparison_pi_infinite_series.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Comparison_pi_infinite_series.svg/600px-Comparison_pi_infinite_series.svg.png 2x" width="300"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Comparison_pi_infinite_series.svg" title="放大"></a></div>比較幾個曾用來計算<span class="texhtml">π</span>的無窮級數的收斂情形。<i>S<sub>n</sub></i>是只取前n項的近似值。每一個圖都是對應前一張圖的陰影部份，然後橫軸放大10倍。<a href="/wiki/File:Comparison_pi_infinite_series.svg" title="File:Comparison pi infinite series.svg">（點擊後可以察看細節）</a></div></div></div>
<p>16世紀及17世紀時，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的計算開始改用<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E7%A9%B7%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="无穷级数">無窮级数</a>的計算方式。無窮级数是一組<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E7%A9%B7%E6%95%B0%E5%88%97" title="无穷数列">無窮數列</a>的和<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-27"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:185–191</sup>。無窮级数讓數學家可以計算出比<a href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E5%9F%BA%E7%B1%B3%E5%BE%B7" title="阿基米德">阿基米德</a>以及其他用幾何方式計算的數學家更準確的結果。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-28"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:185–191</sup>雖然<a href="/wiki/%E8%A9%B9%E5%A7%86%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E6%A0%BC%E9%9B%B7%E6%9E%9C%E9%87%8C" title="詹姆斯·格雷果里">詹姆斯·格雷果里</a>及<a href="/wiki/%E6%88%88%E7%89%B9%E5%BC%97%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E8%8E%B1%E5%B8%83%E5%B0%BC%E8%8C%A8" title="戈特弗里德·莱布尼茨">戈特弗里德·莱布尼茨</a>等歐洲數學家利用無窮數列計算<span class="texhtml">π</span>而使得该方法为大家所知，但这种方法最早是由<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%B0%E5%BA%A6" title="印度">印度</a>科學家在大約1400到1500年之間發現的。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-29"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:185-186</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69"><a href="#cite_note-69">[67]</a></sup>第一個记载的用無窮级数計算<span class="texhtml">π</span>的人是约公元1500年左右时，印度天文學家<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Nilakantha Somayaji" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="尼拉卡莎·薩默亞士"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E6%8B%89%E5%8D%A1%E8%8E%8E%C2%B7%E8%96%A9%E9%BB%98%E4%BA%9E%E5%A3%AB&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="尼拉卡莎·薩默亞士（页面不存在）">尼拉卡莎·薩默亞士</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nilakantha_Somayaji" title="en:Nilakantha Somayaji"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Nilakantha Somayaji</span></a></span>）</span></span>在他的著作《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Tantrasamgraha" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="系統匯編"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%B3%BB%E7%B5%B1%E5%8C%AF%E7%B7%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="系統匯編（页面不存在）">系統匯編</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tantrasamgraha" title="en:Tantrasamgraha"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Tantrasamgraha</span></a></span>）</span></span>》中用梵語詩所記錄。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Roypp_70-0"><a href="#cite_note-Roypp-70">[68]</a></sup>當時沒有這個數列對應的證明，而證明出現在另一本較晚的印度作品《<span class="ilh-all ilh-blue" data-foreign-title="Yuktibhāṣā" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="基本原理"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9F%BA%E6%9C%AC%E5%8E%9F%E7%90%86" title="基本原理">基本原理</a></span></span>》，年代約在公元1530年。尼拉卡莎將該數列歸功於更早期的印度數學家<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Madhava of Sangamagrama" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="桑加馬格拉馬的馬德哈瓦"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%A1%91%E5%8A%A0%E9%A6%AC%E6%A0%BC%E6%8B%89%E9%A6%AC%E7%9A%84%E9%A6%AC%E5%BE%B7%E5%93%88%E7%93%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="桑加馬格拉馬的馬德哈瓦（页面不存在）">桑加馬格拉馬的馬德哈瓦</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Madhava_of_Sangamagrama" title="en:Madhava of Sangamagrama"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Madhava of Sangamagrama</span></a></span>）</span></span>（ 1350 –  1425）。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Roypp_70-1"><a href="#cite_note-Roypp-70">[68]</a></sup>有許多相關的無窮级数，包括有關<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sin }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>sin</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sin }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sin" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ee55beec18afd710e7ab767964b915b020c65093" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.856ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>、<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \tan }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>tan</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \tan }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\tan" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b57c91704d9ab0366a6436869e2968491efc5155" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.36ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>及<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \cos }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\cos" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e473a3de151d75296f141f9f482fe59d582a7509" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.111ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的，現在稱為<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Madhava series" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="馬德哈瓦數列"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%A6%AC%E5%BE%B7%E5%93%88%E7%93%A6%E6%95%B8%E5%88%97&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="馬德哈瓦數列（页面不存在）">馬德哈瓦數列</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Madhava_series" title="en:Madhava series"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Madhava series</span></a></span>）</span></span>或<a href="/wiki/%CE%A0%E7%9A%84%E8%8E%B1%E5%B8%83%E5%B0%BC%E8%8C%A8%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="Π的莱布尼茨公式">π的莱布尼茨公式</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Roypp_70-2"><a href="#cite_note-Roypp-70">[68]</a></sup>。瑪達瓦在1400年用無窮级数計算<span class="texhtml">π</span>到第11位小數，但在1430年一位波斯數學家<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%A1%E8%A5%BF" title="卡西">卡西</a>利用多邊形算法否定了他算的的結果<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-71"><a href="#cite_note-71">[69]</a></sup>。
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:GodfreyKneller-IsaacNewton-1689.jpg"><img alt="長髮艾萨克·牛顿的畫像" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1916" data-file-width="1364" decoding="async" height="239" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/GodfreyKneller-IsaacNewton-1689.jpg/170px-GodfreyKneller-IsaacNewton-1689.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/GodfreyKneller-IsaacNewton-1689.jpg/255px-GodfreyKneller-IsaacNewton-1689.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/GodfreyKneller-IsaacNewton-1689.jpg/340px-GodfreyKneller-IsaacNewton-1689.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:GodfreyKneller-IsaacNewton-1689.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E8%89%BE%E8%90%A8%E5%85%8B%C2%B7%E7%89%9B%E9%A1%BF" title="艾萨克·牛顿">艾萨克·牛顿</a>利用無窮级数計算<span class="texhtml">π</span>到第15位，後來寫道：「我很羞愧的告訴你我為了這個計算用了多少個數字。」<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Newton_72-0"><a href="#cite_note-Newton-72">[70]</a></sup></div></div></div>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9F%A6%E8%BE%BE%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="韦达公式">歐洲第一個發現的無窮項圓周率公式</a>是<a href="/wiki/%E7%84%A1%E7%AA%AE%E4%B9%98%E7%A9%8D" title="無窮乘積">無窮乘積</a>（和一般用來計算<span class="texhtml">π</span>的無窮級數不同），由法國科學家<a href="/wiki/%E5%BC%97%E6%9C%97%E7%B4%A2%E7%93%A6%C2%B7%E9%9F%A6%E8%BE%BE" title="弗朗索瓦·韦达">弗朗索瓦·韦达</a>在1593年發現<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-30"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:187</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73"><a href="#cite_note-73">[71]</a></sup>：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {2}{\pi }}={\frac {\sqrt {2}}{2}}\cdot {\frac {\sqrt {2+{\sqrt {2}}}}{2}}\cdot {\frac {\sqrt {2+{\sqrt {2+{\sqrt {2}}}}}}{2}}\cdots }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {2}{\pi }}={\frac {\sqrt {2}}{2}}\cdot {\frac {\sqrt {2+{\sqrt {2}}}}{2}}\cdot {\frac {\sqrt {2+{\sqrt {2+{\sqrt {2}}}}}}{2}}\cdots }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/471259d8063f909988b7457a3e2d9c62f73efb01" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:42.518ex; height:9.009ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E7%B4%84%E7%BF%B0%C2%B7%E6%B2%83%E5%88%A9%E6%96%AF" title="約翰·沃利斯">約翰·沃利斯</a>在1655年發現了<a href="/wiki/%E6%B2%83%E5%88%A9%E6%96%AF%E4%B9%98%E7%A7%AF" title="沃利斯乘积">沃利斯乘积</a>，是歐洲第二個發現的無窮項圓周率公式<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-31"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:187</sup>：
</p>

<p><a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AD%A6" title="微积分学">微积分学</a>是由英國科學家<a href="/wiki/%E8%89%BE%E8%90%A8%E5%85%8B%C2%B7%E7%89%9B%E9%A1%BF" title="艾萨克·牛顿">艾萨克·牛顿</a>及德國數學家<a href="/wiki/%E6%88%88%E7%89%B9%E5%BC%97%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E8%8E%B1%E5%B8%83%E5%B0%BC%E8%8C%A8" title="戈特弗里德·莱布尼茨">戈特弗里德·莱布尼茨</a>在1660年代發明，因此也出現許多計算<span class="texhtml">π</span>的無窮級數。牛頓自己就利用<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8D%E6%AD%A3%E5%BC%A6" title="反正弦">反正弦</a>（<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \arcsin }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>arcsin</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \arcsin }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \arcsin }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/627fcadc0495786c9167c5487a1a795bb1940edd" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.962ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>）數列在1655年或1666年將<span class="texhtml">π</span>近似到第15位小數，後來寫到「我很羞愧的告訴你我為了這個計算用了多少個數字，我當時沒有做其他的事。」<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Newton_72-1"><a href="#cite_note-Newton-72">[70]</a></sup>
</p><p>蘇格蘭數學家<a href="/wiki/%E8%A9%B9%E5%A7%86%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E6%A0%BC%E9%9B%B7%E6%9E%9C%E9%87%8C" title="詹姆斯·格雷果里">詹姆斯·格雷果里</a>在1671年發現了馬德哈瓦公式，莱布尼茨也在1674年發現：<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-32"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:188–189</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LS_74-0"><a href="#cite_note-LS-74">[72]</a></sup>
</p>

</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E7%B4%84%E7%BF%B0%C2%B7%E6%A2%85%E6%AC%BD" title="約翰·梅欽">約翰·梅欽</a>在1706年利用格雷果里-莱布尼茨級數產生了一個可以快速收斂的公式：<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-35"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:192–193</sup>
</p>

<p>梅欽用這個公式計算到<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的第100位小數<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-36"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:72–74</sup>後來其他數學家也發展了一些類似公式，現在稱為<a href="/wiki/%E6%A2%85%E6%AC%BD%E9%A1%9E%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="梅欽類公式">梅欽類公式</a>，創下了許多計算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>位數的記錄。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-37"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:72–74</sup>在進入電腦時代時，梅欽類公式仍然是个耳熟能详的可以計算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的公式，而且在约250年的时间里，很多有關<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>位數的記錄都是梅欽類公式所得，比如在1946年時由達尼爾·弗格森（<span lang="en">Daniel Ferguson</span>）用這類公式計算到第620位小數，是在沒有計算設備輔助下的最佳紀錄。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-38"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:192–196, 205</sup>
</p><p>1844年，計算天才<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Zacharias Dase" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="扎卡里亞斯·達斯"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%89%8E%E5%8D%A1%E9%87%8C%E4%BA%9E%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E9%81%94%E6%96%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="扎卡里亞斯·達斯（页面不存在）">扎卡里亞斯·達斯</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zacharias_Dase" title="en:Zacharias Dase"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Zacharias Dase</span></a></span>）</span></span>在德國數學家<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%A1%E7%88%BE%C2%B7%E5%BC%97%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%B7%E9%87%8C%E5%B8%8C%C2%B7%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF" title="卡爾·弗里德里希·高斯">卡爾·弗里德里希·高斯</a>的要求下以梅欽類公式心算了<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的200個小數位，並創下紀錄。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-39"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:194-196</sup>英國數學家<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="William Shanks" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="威廉·謝克斯"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A8%81%E5%BB%89%C2%B7%E8%AC%9D%E5%85%8B%E6%96%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="威廉·謝克斯（页面不存在）">威廉·謝克斯</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shanks" title="en:William Shanks"><span dir="auto" lang="en">William Shanks</span></a></span>）</span></span>花了15年的時間計算<span class="texhtml">π</span>到小數707位，不過中間在第528位小數時出錯，因此後面的小數也都不正確。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-40"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:194–196</sup>
</p>
<h4><span id=".E6.94.B6.E6.95.9B.E9.80.9F.E5.BA.A6"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="收敛速度">收敛速度</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="编辑章节：收敛速度">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>有些<span class="texhtml">π</span>的無窮級數<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%94%B6%E6%96%82%E7%B4%9A%E6%95%B8" title="收斂級數">收斂</a>的比其他級數要快，數學家一般會選用收斂速度較快的級數，可以在較少的計算量下計算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>，且達到需要的準確度<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Aconverge_75-0"><a href="#cite_note-Aconverge-75">[73]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-41"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:15–17, 70–72, 104, 156, 192–197, 201–202</sup>。以下是<span class="texhtml">π</span>的<a href="/wiki/%CE%A0%E7%9A%84%E8%8E%B1%E5%B8%83%E5%B0%BC%E8%8C%A8%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="Π的莱布尼茨公式">莱布尼茨公式</a>：<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-42"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:69–72</sup>
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi ={\frac {4}{1}}-{\frac {4}{3}}+{\frac {4}{5}}-{\frac {4}{7}}+{\frac {4}{9}}-{\frac {4}{11}}+{\frac {4}{13}}-\cdots }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>隨著一項一項的值加入總和中，只要項次夠多，總和最後會慢慢接近<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>

</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的第五小數<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76"><a href="#cite_note-76">[74]</a></sup>。
</p><p>尼拉卡莎在15世紀發展了另一個<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>

<p>計算前5項後，格雷果里-萊布尼茨級數的和跟<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的誤差為0.2，而尼拉卡莎級數和的誤差為0.002。尼拉卡莎級數收斂的快很多，因此也比較適合用來計算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的數值。收斂更快的級數有<a href="/wiki/%E6%A2%85%E6%AC%BD%E9%A1%9E%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="梅欽類公式">梅欽類公式</a>及<a href="/wiki/%E6%A5%9A%E5%BE%B7%E8%AF%BA%E5%A4%AB%E6%96%AF%E5%9F%BA%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95" title="楚德诺夫斯基算法">楚德诺夫斯基算法</a>，後者每計算一項就可以得到14位正確的小數值數<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Aconverge_75-1"><a href="#cite_note-Aconverge-75">[73]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.97.A0.E7.90.86.E6.80.A7.E4.B8.8E.E8.B6.85.E8.B6.8A.E6.80.A7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="无理性与超越性">无理性与超越性</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="编辑章节：无理性与超越性">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">参见：<a href="/wiki/%E6%9E%97%E5%BE%B7%E6%9B%BC-%E9%AD%8F%E5%B0%94%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%E6%8B%89%E6%96%AF%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="林德曼-魏尔斯特拉斯定理">林德曼-魏尔斯特拉斯定理</a></div>
<p>并非所有和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>有关的研究都旨在提高计算它的准确性。1735年，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89" title="欧拉">欧拉</a>解决了<a href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B4%E5%A1%9E%E5%B0%94%E9%97%AE%E9%A2%98" title="巴塞尔问题">巴塞尔问题</a>，因而建立了所有<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E5%80%92%E6%95%B8" title="平方倒數">平方数倒数</a>和与<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>

<semantics>

</mrow>

<p>1761年，瑞士数学家<a href="/wiki/%E7%BA%A6%E7%BF%B0%C2%B7%E6%B5%B7%E5%9B%A0%E9%87%8C%E5%B8%8C%C2%B7%E6%9C%97%E4%BC%AF" title="约翰·海因里希·朗伯">约翰·海因里希·朗伯</a>利用<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E5%88%87%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="正切函数">正切函数</a>的无穷连分数表达式<a href="/wiki/%E8%AF%81%E6%98%8E%CF%80%E6%98%AF%E6%97%A0%E7%90%86%E6%95%B0" title="证明π是无理数">证明</a>了<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>超越性猜想。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-44"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:196</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80"><a href="#cite_note-80">[78]</a></sup><a href="/wiki/%E6%88%88%E5%BC%97%E9%9B%B7%C2%B7%E5%93%88%E7%BD%97%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E5%93%88%E4%BB%A3" title="戈弗雷·哈罗德·哈代">哈代</a>在其著作《数论导引》中则称此证明在提出後，經過<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B8%8C%E5%B0%94%E4%BC%AF%E7%89%B9" title="希尔伯特">希尔伯特</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%96%BD%E7%93%A6%E5%85%B9" title="施瓦兹">施瓦兹</a>和其他一些人化简过。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-81"><a href="#cite_note-81">[79]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id=".CF.80.E7.AC.A6.E5.8F.B7.E7.9A.84.E5.BC.95.E5.85.A5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="π符号的引入"><span class="texhtml">π</span>符号的引入</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="编辑章节：π符号的引入">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Leonhard_Euler_2.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="767" data-file-width="614" decoding="async" height="212" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Leonhard_Euler_2.jpg/170px-Leonhard_Euler_2.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Leonhard_Euler_2.jpg/255px-Leonhard_Euler_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Leonhard_Euler_2.jpg/340px-Leonhard_Euler_2.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Leonhard_Euler_2.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E8%90%8A%E6%98%82%E5%93%88%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E6%AD%90%E6%8B%89" title="萊昂哈德·歐拉">萊昂哈德·歐拉</a>在他在1736年到1748年的作品中開始使用希臘字母<span class="texhtml">π</span>表示圓周率，因此也開始廣為數學界使用</div></div></div>
<p>在用<span class="texhtml">π</span>专指“圆周率”之前，希腊字母即已用於幾何概念中<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-45"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:166</sup>。<a href="/wiki/%E5%A8%81%E5%BB%89%C2%B7%E5%A5%A5%E7%89%B9%E9%9B%B7%E5%BE%B7" title="威廉·奥特雷德">威廉·奥特雷德</a>在1647年起在《數學之鑰》（Clavis Mathematicae）就已經用<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>及<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \delta }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>δ<!-- δ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \delta }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\delta " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c5321cfa797202b3e1f8620663ff43c4660ea03a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.049ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>（對應p和d的希臘字母）來表示圓的周長及直徑的比例。
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E5%A8%81%E5%BB%89%C2%B7%E7%90%BC%E6%96%AF_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E5%AE%B6)" title="威廉·琼斯 (数学家)">威廉·琼斯</a>在他1706年出版的《新數學導論》（<span lang="en">A New Introduction to the Mathematics</span>）中提到了<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>，是目前已知最早专门用希臘字母<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>表示圓周和其直徑比例的人<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82"><a href="#cite_note-82">[80]</a></sup>。這個希臘字母的第一次出现，是在书中討論一個半徑為1的圓時，提到「其圓周長的一半（<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>）」。琼斯選用了<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的原因可能是因為它是希臘文中“周边”一词“<span lang="el">περιφέρεια</span>”的第一個字<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83"><a href="#cite_note-83">[81]</a></sup>。不過琼斯提到，他的那些有關<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的算式是出自「真正聰明的約翰·梅欽先生」，因此人们推測在瓊斯之前，<a href="/wiki/%E7%B4%84%E7%BF%B0%C2%B7%E6%A2%85%E6%AC%BD" title="約翰·梅欽">約翰·梅欽</a>就已经开始使用此希臘字母表示圓周率<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-46"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:166</sup>。
</p><p>瓊斯是在1706年開始使用此希臘字母，但直到<a href="/wiki/%E8%90%8A%E6%98%82%E5%93%88%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E6%AD%90%E6%8B%89" title="萊昂哈德·歐拉">萊昂哈德·歐拉</a>在其1736年出版的《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Mechanica" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="力學 (書籍)"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8A%9B%E5%AD%B8_(%E6%9B%B8%E7%B1%8D)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="力學 (書籍)（页面不存在）">力學</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mechanica" title="en:Mechanica"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Mechanica</span></a></span>）</span></span>》中開始使用之后，其他的数学家们才纷纷开始用<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>来指代圆周率。在此之前，數字家可能用像<i>c</i>或<i>p</i>之類的字母代表圓周率<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-47"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:166</sup>。因為歐拉與歐洲其他數學家之间时常互相写信来往，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h2><span id=".E7.8E.B0.E4.BB.A3.E6.95.B0.E5.80.BC.E8.BF.91.E4.BC.BC"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="现代数值近似">现代数值近似</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="编辑章节：现代数值近似">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E8.AE.A1.E7.AE.97.E6.9C.BA.E6.97.B6.E4.BB.A3.E4.B8.8E.E8.BF.AD.E4.BB.A3.E7.AE.97.E6.B3.95"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="计算机时代与迭代算法">计算机时代与迭代算法</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="编辑章节：计算机时代与迭代算法">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:JohnvonNeumann-LosAlamos.gif"><img alt="一位穿著西裝男士的照片" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="639" data-file-width="490" decoding="async" height="222" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/JohnvonNeumann-LosAlamos.gif/170px-JohnvonNeumann-LosAlamos.gif" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/JohnvonNeumann-LosAlamos.gif/255px-JohnvonNeumann-LosAlamos.gif 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/JohnvonNeumann-LosAlamos.gif/340px-JohnvonNeumann-LosAlamos.gif 2x" width="170"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:JohnvonNeumann-LosAlamos.gif" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E7%BA%A6%E7%BF%B0%C2%B7%E5%86%AF%C2%B7%E8%AF%BA%E4%BC%8A%E6%9B%BC" title="约翰·冯·诺伊曼">约翰·冯·诺伊曼</a>所在的團隊是第一個用數位計算機<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E5%AD%90%E6%95%B8%E5%80%BC%E7%A9%8D%E5%88%86%E8%A8%88%E7%AE%97%E6%A9%9F" title="電子數值積分計算機">ENIAC</a>來計算<span class="texhtml">π</span>的</div></div></div>

<p>則<span class="texhtml">π</span>的估計值為

<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \scriptstyle \pi \approx {\frac {(a_{n}+b_{n})^{2}}{4t_{n}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
