<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \scriptstyle \pi \approx {\frac {(a_{n}+b_{n})^{2}}{4t_{n}}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \scriptstyle \pi \approx {\frac {(a_{n}+b_{n})^{2}}{4t_{n}}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9fbdf5841be34f375e64b3165ea92230afcdd604" style="vertical-align: -1.338ex; width:9.081ex; height:4.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl></div></div>
<p>二十世紀中期计算机技术的发展、革新再次引发了計算<span class="texhtml">π</span>位數的熱潮。美國數學家<a href="/wiki/%E7%BA%A6%E7%BF%B0%C2%B7%E4%BC%A6%E5%A5%87" title="约翰·伦奇">约翰·伦奇</a>及李維·史密斯在1949年利用桌上型計算機計算到1,120位<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-50"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:205</sup>。同年，喬治·韋斯納（George Reitwiesner）及<a href="/wiki/%E7%BA%A6%E7%BF%B0%C2%B7%E5%86%AF%C2%B7%E8%AF%BA%E4%BC%8A%E6%9B%BC" title="约翰·冯·诺伊曼">约翰·冯·诺伊曼</a>帶領的團隊利用<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8D%E4%B8%89%E8%A7%92%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="反三角函数">反三角函数</a>（arctan）的無窮級數，通过<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E5%AD%90%E6%95%B8%E5%80%BC%E7%A9%8D%E5%88%86%E8%A8%88%E7%AE%97%E6%A9%9F" title="電子數值積分計算機">ENIAC</a>計算到了小數第2,037位，花了70小時的電腦工作時間<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84"><a href="#cite_note-84">[82]</a></sup>。這一紀錄後來多次由其他透過arctan級數计算出的結果打破（1957年到7480位小數，1958年到第一萬位數，1961年到第十萬位小數），直到1973年，人们计算出了小数点后的第一百萬位小數<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-51"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:197</sup>。
</p><p>1980年代的两项發明加速了<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的計算。第一项是人们發现了新的的迭代法去计算<span class="texhtml">π</span>的值，其計算速度比無窮級數會要快很多。另一项是人们發现了可以快速計算大數字乘積的<a href="/wiki/%E4%B9%98%E6%B3%95%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95" title="乘法算法">乘法演算法</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-52"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:15–17</sup>。這類演算法在現代<span class="texhtml">π</span>的計算上格外的重要，因為電腦大部分的工作時間都是在計算乘法<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-53"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:131</sup>。這類演算法包括<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Karatsuba%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95" title="Karatsuba算法">Karatsuba算法</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Toom%E2%80%93Cook%E4%B9%98%E6%B3%95" title="Toom–Cook乘法">Toom–Cook乘法</a>及以<a href="/wiki/%E5%82%85%E9%87%8C%E5%8F%B6%E5%8F%98%E6%8D%A2" title="傅里叶变换">傅里叶变换</a>為基礎的乘法演算法（傅里叶乘法）<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-54"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:132, 140</sup>。
</p><p>迭代演算法最早是在1975年至1976年间分别由美國物理學家<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Eugene Salamin (mathematician)" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="尤金·薩拉明"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%A4%E9%87%91%C2%B7%E8%96%A9%E6%8B%89%E6%98%8E&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="尤金·薩拉明（页面不存在）">尤金·薩拉明</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eugene_Salamin_(mathematician)" title="en:Eugene Salamin (mathematician)"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Eugene Salamin (mathematician)</span></a></span>）</span></span>及奧地利科學家<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Richard Brent (scientist)" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="理查·布蘭特"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%90%86%E6%9F%A5%C2%B7%E5%B8%83%E8%98%AD%E7%89%B9&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="理查·布蘭特（页面不存在）">理查·布蘭特</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Richard_Brent_(scientist)" title="en:Richard Brent (scientist)"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Richard Brent (scientist)</span></a></span>）</span></span>独立提出<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-55"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:87</sup>。這两个演算法没有依赖無窮級數來計算。迭代會重覆一個特定的計算，将前一次的計算結果作为這一次的輸入值，使得計算結果漸漸的趨近理想值。此方式的原始版本其實是在160年前由<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%A1%E7%88%BE%C2%B7%E5%BC%97%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%B7%E9%87%8C%E5%B8%8C%C2%B7%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF" title="卡爾·弗里德里希·高斯">卡爾·弗里德里希·高斯</a>提出，現在稱為<a href="/wiki/%E7%AE%97%E6%9C%AF-%E5%87%A0%E4%BD%95%E5%B9%B3%E5%9D%87%E6%95%B0" title="算术-几何平均数">算术-几何平均数算法</a>（AGM法）或<a href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF-%E5%8B%92%E8%AE%A9%E5%BE%B7%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95" title="高斯-勒让德算法">高斯-勒让德算法</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-56"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:87</sup>。因為薩拉明及布蘭特都曾对此進行修改，因此这个算法也稱為薩拉明-布蘭特演算法。
</p><p>迭代演算法因為收斂速度比無窮級數快很多，在1980年代以後廣為使用。無窮級數隨著項次的增加，一般來說正確的位數也會增加幾位，但迭代演算法每多一次計算，正確的位數會呈几何级数增长。例如薩拉明-布蘭特演算法每多一次計算，正確位數會是之前的二倍。1984年加拿大人<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Jonathan Borwein" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="喬納森·波温"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%96%AC%E7%B4%8D%E6%A3%AE%C2%B7%E6%B3%A2%E6%B8%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="喬納森·波温（页面不存在）">喬納森·波温</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jonathan_Borwein" title="en:Jonathan Borwein"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Jonathan Borwein</span></a></span>）</span></span>及<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Peter Borwein" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="彼得·波温"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BD%BC%E5%BE%97%C2%B7%E6%B3%A2%E6%B8%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="彼得·波温（页面不存在）">彼得·波温</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peter_Borwein" title="en:Peter Borwein"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Peter Borwein</span></a></span>）</span></span>提出一個迭代演算法，每多一次計算，正確位數會是之前的四倍，1987年時有另一個迭代演算法，每多一次計算，正確位數會是之前的五倍<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-85"><a href="#cite_note-85">[83]</a></sup>。日本數學家<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%91%E7%94%B0%E5%BA%B7%E6%AD%A3" title="金田康正">金田康正</a>使用的演算法在1955年及2002年之間創下了若干个紀錄<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Background_86-0"><a href="#cite_note-Background-86">[84]</a></sup>。不過迭代演算法的快速收斂也有其代價，因为这个算法需要的内存的大小明顯的要比無窮級數要多<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Background_86-1"><a href="#cite_note-Background-86">[84]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.AE.A1.E7.AE.97.CF.80.E7.9A.84.E6.84.8F.E4.B9.89"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="计算π的意义">计算<span class="texhtml">π</span>的意义</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="编辑章节：计算π的意义">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:402px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Record_pi_approximations.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="528" data-file-width="1024" decoding="async" height="206" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/25/Record_pi_approximations.svg/400px-Record_pi_approximations.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/25/Record_pi_approximations.svg/600px-Record_pi_approximations.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/25/Record_pi_approximations.svg/800px-Record_pi_approximations.svg.png 2x" width="400"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Record_pi_approximations.svg" title="放大"></a></div>當數學家發現新的算法、電腦變得普及时，<span class="texhtml">π</span>的已知小數位急剧增加。注意垂直坐标使用了<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%B9%E6%95%B0" title="对数">对数坐标</a>。</div></div></div>
<p>一般而言，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>值并不需要过于精确便能够满足大部分的数学运算的需求。按照約爾格·阿恩特（Jörg Arndt）及克里斯托夫·黑內爾（<span lang="en">Christoph Haenel</span>）的计算，39個數位已足夠運算絕大多數的<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%87%E5%AE%99%E5%AD%A6" title="宇宙学">宇宙学</a>的计算需求，因為這個精確度已能夠将<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%AF%E8%A7%80%E6%B8%AC%E5%AE%87%E5%AE%99" title="可觀測宇宙">可觀測宇宙</a>圆周的精确度準確至一個原子大小<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_b_87-0"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt_b-87">[85]</a></sup>。
尽管如此，人們仍然是奋力地運算出<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>小数点后的上千甚至上百萬個數位<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-57"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:17–19</sup>。這一部分是出于人類對打破記錄的冲动，因为那些和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>有關的成就往往成為世界各地的新聞頭條<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-msnbc.msn.com_88-0"><a href="#cite_note-msnbc.msn.com-88">[86]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-independent.co.uk_89-0"><a href="#cite_note-independent.co.uk-89">[87]</a></sup>。此外，这其中也有一些實際的好處，例如測試<a href="/wiki/%E8%B6%85%E7%BA%A7%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97%E6%9C%BA" title="超级计算机">超级计算机</a>、測試数值分析算法等（包括<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Multiplication algorithm#Fast multiplication algorithms for large inputs" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="Multiplication algorithm#Fast multiplication algorithms for large inputs"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Multiplication_algorithm&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Multiplication algorithm（页面不存在）">高精度乘法算法</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Multiplication_algorithm#Fast_multiplication_algorithms_for_large_inputs" title="en:Multiplication algorithm"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Multiplication algorithm#Fast multiplication algorithms for large inputs</span></a></span>）</span></span>）。在純粹數學的领域中，计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的位数也能让人们来评定<span class="texhtml">π</span>的隨機性<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-58"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:18</sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.BF.AB.E9.80.9F.E6.94.B6.E6.95.9B.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="快速收敛级数">快速收敛级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="编辑章节：快速收敛级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Srinivasa_Ramanujan_-_OPC_-_1.jpg"><img alt="一位男士的肖像" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1315" data-file-width="960" decoding="async" height="233" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Srinivasa_Ramanujan_-_OPC_-_1.jpg/170px-Srinivasa_Ramanujan_-_OPC_-_1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Srinivasa_Ramanujan_-_OPC_-_1.jpg/255px-Srinivasa_Ramanujan_-_OPC_-_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Srinivasa_Ramanujan_-_OPC_-_1.jpg/340px-Srinivasa_Ramanujan_-_OPC_-_1.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Srinivasa_Ramanujan_-_OPC_-_1.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E6%96%AF%E9%87%8C%E5%B0%BC%E7%93%A6%E7%91%9F%C2%B7%E6%8B%89%E9%A9%AC%E5%8A%AA%E9%87%91" title="斯里尼瓦瑟·拉马努金">斯里尼瓦瑟·拉马努金</a>的肖像，他在印度独立工作时提出了许多新颖的计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的数列。</div></div></div>
<p>现代计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的程序不仅仅局限于迭代算法。20世纪80与90年代，人们发现了一些可用来计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的新无穷级数，其收敛速度可与迭代算法媲美，而又有着复杂度、内存密集度更低的优势。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Background_86-2"><a href="#cite_note-Background-86">[84]</a></sup>印度数学家<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%AF%E9%87%8C%E5%B0%BC%E7%93%A6%E7%91%9F%C2%B7%E6%8B%89%E9%A9%AC%E5%8A%AA%E9%87%91" title="斯里尼瓦瑟·拉马努金">斯里尼瓦瑟·拉马努金</a>是这方面的先驱，他在1914年发表了许多与<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>相关的公式，这些公式十分新颖，极为优雅而又颇具数学深度，收敛速度也非常快。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-59"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:103–104</sup>下式即为一例，其中用到了<a href="/wiki/%E6%A8%A1%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B" title="模方程">模方程</a>：
</p>

<p>这个无穷级数收敛速度远快于绝大多数反正切数列，包括梅钦公式。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-60"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:104</sup>第一位使用拉马努金公式计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>并取得进展的是<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Bill Gosper" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="比尔·高斯珀"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%AF%94%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF%E7%8F%80&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="比尔·高斯珀（页面不存在）">比尔·高斯珀</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bill_Gosper" title="en:Bill Gosper"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Bill Gosper</span></a></span>）</span></span>，他在1985年算得了小数点后一千七百万位。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-61"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:104, 206</sup>拉马努金公式开创了现代数值近似算法的先河，此后波尔文兄弟和<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Chudnovsky brothers" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="楚德诺夫斯基兄弟"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%A5%9A%E5%BE%B7%E8%AF%BA%E5%A4%AB%E6%96%AF%E5%9F%BA%E5%85%84%E5%BC%9F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="楚德诺夫斯基兄弟（页面不存在）">楚德诺夫斯基兄弟</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chudnovsky_brothers" title="en:Chudnovsky brothers"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Chudnovsky brothers</span></a></span>）</span></span>进一步发展了这类算法。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-62"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:110–111</sup>后者于1987年提出了<a href="/wiki/%E6%A5%9A%E5%BE%B7%E8%AF%BA%E5%A4%AB%E6%96%AF%E5%9F%BA%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95" title="楚德诺夫斯基算法">楚德诺夫斯基公式</a>，如下所示：

<p>此公式每计算一项就能得到<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的约14位数值<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90"><a href="#cite_note-90">[88]</a></sup>，因而用於突破圆周率的数位的计算。利用这个公式，楚德诺夫斯基兄弟于1989年算得<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>小数点后10亿（10<sup>9</sup>）位，<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%95%E5%B8%83%E9%87%8C%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E8%B4%9D%E6%8B%89" title="法布里斯·贝拉">法布里斯·贝拉</a>于2009年算得2.7千亿（2.7×10<sup>12</sup>）位，亚历山大·易和近藤滋在2011年算得一万亿（10<sup>13</sup>）位。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-63"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:110–111, 206</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91"><a href="#cite_note-91">[89]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NW_92-0"><a href="#cite_note-NW-92">[90]</a></sup>类似的公式还有<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Ramanujan–Sato series" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="拉马努金-佐藤级数"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%8B%89%E9%A9%AC%E5%8A%AA%E9%87%91-%E4%BD%90%E8%97%A4%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="拉马努金-佐藤级数（页面不存在）">拉马努金-佐藤级数</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ramanujan%E2%80%93Sato_series" title="en:Ramanujan–Sato series"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Ramanujan–Sato series</span></a></span>）</span></span>。
</p><p>2006年，加拿大数学家<a href="/wiki/%E8%A5%BF%E8%92%99%C2%B7%E6%99%AE%E5%8B%9E%E5%A4%AB" title="西蒙·普勞夫">西蒙·普勞夫</a>利用PSLQ<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="integer relation algorithm" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="整数关系算法"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%95%B4%E6%95%B0%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="整数关系算法（页面不存在）">整数关系算法</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/integer_relation_algorithm" title="en:integer relation algorithm"><span dir="auto" lang="en">integer relation algorithm</span></a></span>）</span></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93"><a href="#cite_note-93">[91]</a></sup>按照以下模版生成了几个计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的新公式：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi ^{k}=\sum _{n=1}^{\infty }{\frac {1}{n^{k}}}\left({\frac {a}{q^{n}-1}}+{\frac {b}{q^{2n}-1}}+{\frac {c}{q^{4n}-1}}\right),}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \pi ^{k}=\sum _{n=1}^{\infty }{\frac {1}{n^{k}}}\left({\frac {a}{q^{n}-1}}+{\frac {b}{q^{2n}-1}}+{\frac {c}{q^{4n}-1}}\right),}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/948b735a39a1bbf9a39ba0b6bd7dc63bddcd4351" style="vertical-align: -3.005ex; width:46.161ex; height:6.843ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle q}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>q</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle q}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="q" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/06809d64fa7c817ffc7e323f85997f783dbdf71d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.07ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>为<a href="/wiki/E%E7%9A%84%CF%80%E6%AC%A1%E6%96%B9" title="E的π次方"><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml">e</span></span><sup><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span></sup></a>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle k}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="k" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c3c9a2c7b599b37105512c5d570edc034056dd40" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.211ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>是一个<a href="/wiki/%E5%A5%87%E5%81%B6%E6%80%A7_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="奇偶性 (数学)">奇数</a>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a,b,c}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mo>,</mo>
<mi>b</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mi>c</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a,b,c}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a,b,c" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f13f068df656c1b1911ae9f81628c49a6181194d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:5.302ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>是普勞夫计算出的有理常数。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94"><a href="#cite_note-94">[92]</a></sup>

<h3><span id=".E8.92.99.E7.89.B9.E5.8D.A1.E6.B4.9B.E6.96.B9.E6.B3.95"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="蒙特卡洛方法">蒙特卡洛方法</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="编辑章节：蒙特卡洛方法">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

.thumbcaption{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .trow>.thumbcaption{text-align:center}}</style><div class="thumb tmulti tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:274px;max-width:274px"><div href="/wiki/File:Pi_30K.gif"><img alt="大量的点随机的散落在一个内切四分之一圆的正方形内" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="500" decoding="async" height="100" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Pi_30K.gif/200px-Pi_30K.gif 2x" width="100"/></a></div><div class="thumbcaption">随机地往内切四分之一圆的正方形内抛掷大量的点。</div></div></div><div class="trow" style="display:flex"><div class="thumbcaption"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%92%99%E7%89%B9%E5%8D%A1%E6%B4%9B%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95" title="蒙特卡洛方法">蒙特卡洛方法</a>基于随机试验结果计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的近似值</div></div></div></div>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%92%99%E7%89%B9%E5%8D%A1%E6%B4%9B%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95" title="蒙特卡洛方法">蒙特卡洛方法</a>是以概率统计理论为指导的一类非常重要的数值计算方法，通过进行大量重复试验计算事件发生的频率，按照<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A7%E6%95%B0%E5%AE%9A%E5%BE%8B" title="大数定律">大数定律</a>（即当试验次数充分大时，频率充分地接近于概率）可以求得<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的近似值<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95"><a href="#cite_note-95">[93]</a></sup>。 <a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%83%E8%B1%90%E6%8A%95%E9%87%9D%E5%95%8F%E9%A1%8C" title="布豐投針問題">布豐投針問題</a>就是其中一个应用的例子：当一枚长度为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle l}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>l</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle l}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="l" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/829091f745070b9eb97a80244129025440a1cfac" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.693ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的针随机地往一个画满间距为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle t\left(l\leq t\right)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>t</mi>

<mo>(</mo>
<mrow>
<mi>l</mi>
<mo>≤<!-- ≤ --></mo>
<mi>t</mi>
</mrow>
<mo>)</mo>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle t\left(l\leq t\right)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle t\left(l\leq t\right)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1e68ad5d1693bdcdeccd43a012bc765e16aa6b03" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:7.667ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>的平行线的平面上抛掷<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>次， 如果针与平行直线相交了<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle m}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>m</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle m}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="m" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a07d98bb302f3856cbabc47b2b9016692e3f7bc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.04ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>次，那么当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>充分大时就可根据以下公式算出<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的近似值<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96"><a href="#cite_note-96">[94]</a></sup>：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi \approx {\frac {2n\ell }{mt}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mi>n</mi>
<mi>ℓ<!-- ℓ --></mi>

</mrow>

</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi \approx {\frac {2n\ell }{mt}}}</annotation>
</semantics>

<p>另一个利用蒙特卡罗方法计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>值的例子是随机地往内切四分之一圆的正方形内抛掷大量的点，落在四分之一圆内的点的数量与抛掷点的总量的比值会近似等于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {\pi }{4}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
<mn>4</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {\pi }{4}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\frac {\pi }{4}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1f89d7c88c1c93dce69a46052a8e276e231063de" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:2.168ex; height:4.676ex;"/></span>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-64"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:39–40</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97"><a href="#cite_note-97">[95]</a></sup>
</p><p><br/>
此外，还可以通过进行<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9A%8F%E6%9C%BA%E6%B8%B8%E8%B5%B0" title="随机游走">随机游走</a>试验，并利用蒙特卡罗方法计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>值，如抛掷一枚均匀的硬币<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle N}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>N</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle N}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="N" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f5e3890c981ae85503089652feb48b191b57aae3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.064ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>次，并记录正面朝上的次数，所得结果中，正面朝上的次数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n_{N}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>n</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>N</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n_{N}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle n_{N}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d6bd843e0734b300c18afdfc25e4927d52038f46" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:3.086ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>服从<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BA%8C%E9%A0%85%E5%88%86%E4%BD%88" title="二項分佈">二項分佈</a>且
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \Pr(n_{N}=m)={\binom {N}{m}}({\frac {1}{2}})^{m}({\frac {1}{2}})^{N-m}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo form="prefix" movablelimits="true">Pr</mo>

<p>因为硬币均匀，所以<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml">N</span></span>次试验中每次试验结果相互独立。由此可定义一系列独立的<a href="/wiki/%E9%9A%8F%E6%9C%BA%E5%8F%98%E9%87%8F" title="随机变量">随机变量</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle X_{k}\left(k=1,2,\ldots \right)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>设<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml">k</span></span>为“硬币正面朝上的次数”减去“硬币反面朝上的次数”，即可得到<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle m-\left(N-m\right)=k}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>并且当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle N}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>

<p>和其他计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的估值已经精确到了第几位。因此，当追求速度或精度时，蒙特卡洛方法不适合用来估计<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<h3><span id=".E9.98.80.E9.97.A8.E7.AE.97.E6.B3.95"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="阀门算法">阀门算法</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="编辑章节：阀门算法">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>1995年引入的兩個算法开辟了研究<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的新途径。因为每计算出一位数字，該數就会像流过阀门的水一样不会再出现在后续的计算过程中，这种新進算法叫做<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="spigot algorithm" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="阀门算法"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%98%80%E9%97%A8%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="阀门算法（页面不存在）">阀门算法</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/spigot_algorithm" title="en:spigot algorithm"><span dir="auto" lang="en">spigot algorithm</span></a></span>）</span></span>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-66"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:77–84</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Gibbons_101-0"><a href="#cite_note-Gibbons-101">[99]</a></sup>这就与无穷级数及迭代算法形成对比——无穷级数和迭代算法自始至终的每一步计算都会涉及到之前所有步骤计算出的中间值。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-67"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:77–84</sup>
</p><p>1995年，美國數學家<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Stan Wagon" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="斯坦·瓦格纳"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%96%AF%E5%9D%A6%C2%B7%E7%93%A6%E6%A0%BC%E7%BA%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="斯坦·瓦格纳（页面不存在）">斯坦·瓦格纳</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stan_Wagon" title="en:Stan Wagon"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Stan Wagon</span></a></span>）</span></span>和斯坦利·拉比諾維茨（<span lang="en">Stanley Rabinowitz</span>）发明了一种簡單的阀门算法<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Gibbons_101-1"><a href="#cite_note-Gibbons-101">[99]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-68"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:77</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102"><a href="#cite_note-102">[100]</a></sup>，其運算速度類似arctan演算法，但速度比迭代算法要慢<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-69"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:77</sup>。
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E8%B4%9D%E5%88%A9-%E6%B3%A2%E5%B0%94%E6%B8%A9-%E6%99%AE%E5%8A%B3%E5%A4%AB%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="贝利-波尔温-普劳夫公式">贝利-波尔温-普劳夫公式</a>（BBP）是另一個阀门算法，屬於一种<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="digit extraction algorithm" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="位數萃取演算法"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BD%8D%E6%95%B8%E8%90%83%E5%8F%96%E6%BC%94%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="位數萃取演算法（页面不存在）">位數萃取演算法</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/digit_extraction_algorithm" title="en:digit extraction algorithm"><span dir="auto" lang="en">digit extraction algorithm</span></a></span>）</span></span>。1995年，<a href="/wiki/%E8%A5%BF%E8%92%99%C2%B7%E6%99%AE%E5%8B%9E%E5%A4%AB" title="西蒙·普勞夫">西蒙·普勞夫</a>等人發現<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-70"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:117, 126–128</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bbpf_103-0"><a href="#cite_note-bbpf-103">[101]</a></sup>
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi =\sum _{k=0}^{\infty }{\frac {1}{16^{k}}}\left({\frac {4}{8k+1}}-{\frac {2}{8k+4}}-{\frac {1}{8k+5}}-{\frac {1}{8k+6}}\right)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi =\sum _{k=0}^{\infty }{\frac {1}{16^{k}}}\left({\frac {4}{8k+1}}-{\frac {2}{8k+4}}-{\frac {1}{8k+5}}-{\frac {1}{8k+6}}\right)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \pi =\sum _{k=0}^{\infty }{\frac {1}{16^{k}}}\left({\frac {4}{8k+1}}-{\frac {2}{8k+4}}-{\frac {1}{8k+5}}-{\frac {1}{8k+6}}\right)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5be33d7e24e7ab4d284dd957955227fb6faee2d3" style="vertical-align: -3.171ex; width:53.602ex; height:7.009ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>這個公式和其他的公式不同，可以在<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E8%BF%9B%E5%88%B6" title="十六进制">十六进制</a>下計算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的任意位數小數，而不用計算所有前面的小數位數<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-71"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:117, 126–128</sup>。一个十六进制下的数位可计算得到特定一个二进制的数位；想要得到一个<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%AB%E8%BF%9B%E5%88%B6" title="八进制">八进制</a>数位的话，计算一、两个十六进制小數即可。目前也已發現一些這種演算法的變體，不過人们還沒有发现針對十進制、可以快速產生特定位數小數數字的位數萃取演算法<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-104"><a href="#cite_note-104">[102]</a></sup>。位數萃取演算法的一個重要用途是用來確認聲稱是計算到<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>小數位數的新記錄：若有聲稱是新紀錄的計算結果出現，先將十進制的數值轉換到十六進制，再用贝利-波尔温-普劳夫公式，去確認最後的一些位數（用亂數決定），若這些位數都對，人们就能有一定把握认为此計算結果是对的<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NW_92-1"><a href="#cite_note-NW-92">[90]</a></sup>。
</p><p>在1998年到2000年之間，<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%86%E5%B8%83%E5%BC%8F%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97" title="分布式计算">分布式计算</a>計畫<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="PiHex" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="PiHex"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=PiHex&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="PiHex（页面不存在）">PiHex</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/PiHex" title="en:PiHex"><span dir="auto" lang="en">PiHex</span></a></span>）</span></span>利用<a href="/wiki/%E8%B2%9D%E6%8B%89%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="貝拉公式">貝拉公式</a>（贝利-波尔温-普劳夫公式的一種變體）計算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的第10<sup>15</sup>個位，結果是0<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-72"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:20</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105"><a href="#cite_note-105">[103]</a></sup>。在2010年9月，一名<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%85%E8%99%8E" title="雅虎">雅虎</a>員工利用公司的<a href="/wiki/Apache_Hadoop" title="Apache Hadoop">Apache Hadoop</a>應用程式在上千台電腦上計算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>在2×10<sup>15</sup>個数位开始，往后数的256個位，其第2×10<sup>15</sup>個位剛好也是0<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-106"><a href="#cite_note-106">[104]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E7.94.A8.E9.80.94"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="用途">用途</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="编辑章节：用途">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>由于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>与圆密切相关，故它出现在许多<a href="/wiki/%E5%90%AB%E5%9C%86%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87%E7%9A%84%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F%E5%88%97%E8%A1%A8" title="含圆周率的公式列表">几何学和三角学的公式</a>中（特别是与圆、球体和椭圆相关的那些）。 此外，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>也出现在其他学科的重要公式中，比如统计学、物理学，傅立叶分析和数论的公式。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.87.A0.E4.BD.95.E5.AD.A6.E4.B8.8E.E4.B8.89.E8.A7.92.E5.AD.A6"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="几何学与三角学">几何学与三角学</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="编辑章节：几何学与三角学">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Circle_Area.svg"><img alt="圆右上四分之一處覆蓋在正方形下的图。" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="264" data-file-width="264" decoding="async" height="220" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Circle_Area.svg/220px-Circle_Area.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Circle_Area.svg/330px-Circle_Area.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Circle_Area.svg/440px-Circle_Area.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Circle_Area.svg" title="放大"></a></div>圆的面积等于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>上述公式是<a href="/wiki/%E7%90%83_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="球 (数学)"><i>n</i> 维球</a>的体积与其边界（<a href="/wiki/N%E7%BB%B4%E7%90%83%E9%9D%A2" title="N维球面">(<i>n</i>−1) 维球的球面</a>）的表面积的特殊情况，具体将在<a href="#Γ函数与斯特灵公式">后文</a>给出解释。
</p><p>描述由圆产生的图形的周长、面积或体积的<a href="/wiki/%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86" title="积分">定积分</a>通常会涉及到<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".E6.8B.93.E6.89.91.E5.AD.A6"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="拓扑学">拓扑学</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="编辑章节：拓扑学">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Uniform_tiling_73-t2.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="930" data-file-width="935" decoding="async" height="219" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Uniform_tiling_73-t2.png/220px-Uniform_tiling_73-t2.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Uniform_tiling_73-t2.png/330px-Uniform_tiling_73-t2.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Uniform_tiling_73-t2.png/440px-Uniform_tiling_73-t2.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Uniform_tiling_73-t2.png" title="放大"></a></div><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Klein quartic" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="克莱因四次曲面"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%85%8B%E8%8E%B1%E5%9B%A0%E5%9B%9B%E6%AC%A1%E6%9B%B2%E9%9D%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="克莱因四次曲面（页面不存在）">克莱因四次曲面</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Klein_quartic" title="en:Klein quartic"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Klein quartic</span></a></span>）</span></span>的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%95%E5%80%BC%E5%8C%96%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="单值化定理">单值化</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%8F%E6%A0%BC" title="亏格">亏格</a>为3且欧拉特征值为−4的面，作为<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%9E%E5%8A%A0%E8%8E%B1%E5%9C%86%E7%9B%98%E6%A8%A1%E5%9E%8B" title="庞加莱圆盘模型">双曲面</a>与<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Fano plane" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="菲诺平面"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%8F%B2%E8%AF%BA%E5%B9%B3%E9%9D%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="菲诺平面（页面不存在）">菲诺平面</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fano_plane" title="en:Fano plane"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Fano plane</span></a></span>）</span></span>的<a href="/wiki/%E7%A9%BA%E9%96%93%E5%B0%8D%E7%A8%B1%E7%BE%A4" title="空間對稱群">对称群</a><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%83%E5%85%83%E5%9F%9F%E4%B8%8A%E4%BA%8C%E9%98%B6%E6%96%B9%E9%98%B5%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E6%AE%8A%E5%B0%84%E5%BD%B1%E7%BA%BF%E6%80%A7%E7%BE%A4&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="七元域上二阶方阵的特殊射影线性群（页面不存在）">PSL(2,7)</a>的商。根据高斯-博内定理，基本域的双曲面积为8<span class="texhtml">π</span>.</div></div></div>
<p>常数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>出现在将<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="differential geometry of surfaces" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="平面微分几何"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B9%B3%E9%9D%A2%E5%BE%AE%E5%88%86%E5%87%A0%E4%BD%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="平面微分几何（页面不存在）">平面微分几何</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/differential_geometry_of_surfaces" title="en:differential geometry of surfaces"><span dir="auto" lang="en">differential geometry of surfaces</span></a></span>）</span></span>及其<a href="/wiki/%E6%8B%93%E6%89%91%E5%AD%A6" title="拓扑学">拓扑学</a>联系起来的<a href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF-%E5%8D%9A%E5%86%85%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="高斯-博内定理">高斯-博内定理</a>中。具体来说，如果一个<a href="/wiki/%E7%B4%A7%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="紧空间">紧</a>曲面<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml"><i>Σ</i></span></span>的<a href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF%E6%9B%B2%E7%8E%87" title="高斯曲率">高斯曲率</a>为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle K}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \chi (\Sigma )}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mi mathvariant="normal">Σ<!-- Σ --></mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \chi (\Sigma )}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \chi (\Sigma )}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ddcac771209df3d6dceee91261eed8e40c1ace54" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.942ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>是该曲面的<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89%E7%A4%BA%E6%80%A7%E6%95%B0" title="欧拉示性数">欧拉示性数</a>，是一个整数。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-110"><a href="#cite_note-110">[108]</a></sup>例如，一个曲率为1（也就是说其<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="radius of curvature" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="曲率半径"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9B%B2%E7%8E%87%E5%8D%8A%E5%BE%91" title="曲率半徑">曲率半径</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/radius_of_curvature" title="en:radius of curvature"><span dir="auto" lang="en">radius of curvature</span></a></span>）</span></span>也为1，对于球面而言此时的曲率半径与半径重合）的球面<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>S</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="S" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4611d85173cd3b508e67077d4a1252c9c05abca2" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.499ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的表面积。球面的欧拉特征数可以通过其<a href="/wiki/%E5%90%8C%E8%B0%83" title="同调">同源组</a>计算，其结果为2。于是，便得出
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A(S)=\int _{S}1\,dA=2\pi \cdot 2=4\pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>S</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>=</mo>
<msub>
<mo>∫<!-- ∫ --></mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>S</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mn>1</mn>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>d</mi>
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
<mo>⋅<!-- ⋅ --></mo>
<mn>2</mn>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>4</mn>
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A(S)=\int _{S}1\,dA=2\pi \cdot 2=4\pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A(S)=\int _{S}1\,dA=2\pi \cdot 2=4\pi }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f541185019255fc11e6ef909d681e99b9490cf88" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:29.658ex; height:5.676ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>即为半径为1的球面的表面积公式。
</p><p>常数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.90.91.E9.87.8F.E5.88.86.E6.9E.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="向量分析">向量分析</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="编辑章节：向量分析">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:YL10M5sph.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="900" data-file-width="1200" decoding="async" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/YL10M5sph.png/220px-YL10M5sph.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/YL10M5sph.png/330px-YL10M5sph.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/YL10M5sph.png/440px-YL10M5sph.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:YL10M5sph.png" title="放大"></a></div>向量分析的方法可以通过分解成<a href="/wiki/%E7%90%83%E8%B0%90%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="球谐函数">球谐函数</a>来理解（图示）</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E5%90%91%E9%87%8F%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90" title="向量分析">向量分析</a>是与<a href="/wiki/%E5%90%91%E9%87%8F%E5%A0%B4" title="向量場">向量場</a>的性质有关的微积分的分支，并有许多物理应用，例如应用在<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E7%A3%81%E5%AD%A6" title="电磁学">电磁学</a>中。位于三维笛卡尔坐标系原点的点源<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle Q}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>Q</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Q}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="Q" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8752c7023b4b3286800fe3238271bbca681219ed" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.838ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Newtonian potential" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="牛顿位势"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%89%9B%E9%A1%BF%E4%BD%8D%E5%8A%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="牛顿位势（页面不存在）">牛顿位势</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Newtonian_potential" title="en:Newtonian potential"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Newtonian potential</span></a></span>）</span></span>为<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-112"><a href="#cite_note-112">[110]</a></sup>
</p>

<p>表示位于距原点<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \left\vert {\boldsymbol {x}}\right\vert }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbf {E} =-\nabla V.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>特殊情况有<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%93%E4%BB%91%E5%AE%9A%E5%BE%8B" title="库仑定律">库仑定律</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%89%9B%E9%A1%BF%E4%B8%87%E6%9C%89%E5%BC%95%E5%8A%9B%E5%AE%9A%E5%BE%8B" title="牛顿万有引力定律">牛顿万有引力定律</a>。<a href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF%E5%AE%9A%E5%BE%8B" title="高斯定律">高斯定律</a>表明，通过包含原点的任何平滑、简单、封闭、可定向曲面<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>标准形式会将<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 4\pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>高斯定律的结果之一是位势<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle V}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>

<p>通过<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%B7%E7%A7%AF" title="卷积">卷积</a>就能得到物质（或电荷）的更一般分布，给出<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%8A%E6%9D%BE%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B" title="泊松方程">泊松方程</a>

<p>其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \rho }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Spacetime_lattice_analogy.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="469" data-file-width="1260" decoding="async" height="82" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Spacetime_lattice_analogy.svg/220px-Spacetime_lattice_analogy.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Spacetime_lattice_analogy.svg/330px-Spacetime_lattice_analogy.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Spacetime_lattice_analogy.svg/440px-Spacetime_lattice_analogy.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Spacetime_lattice_analogy.svg" title="放大"></a></div>爱因斯坦方程表明，时空的曲率是由其中的物质能量产生的。</div></div></div>
<p>常数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</math></span><img alt="c" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/86a67b81c2de995bd608d5b2df50cd8cd7d92455" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.007ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是真空中的<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%89%E9%80%9F" title="光速">光速</a>，而<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle T_{\mu v}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>T</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>μ<!-- μ --></mi>
<mi>v</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle T_{\mu v}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle T_{\mu v}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/38c5e3e7752c2c83d677c2cc8ca096e294931d6c" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:3.378ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>是<a href="/wiki/%E6%87%89%E5%8A%9B-%E8%83%BD%E9%87%8F%E5%BC%B5%E9%87%8F" title="應力-能量張量">應力-能量張量</a>。爱因斯坦方程的左边是度量张量的拉普拉斯算子的非线性模拟，並化簡（reduce）至在弱域的極限，而右边是分布函数的模拟乘以<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 8\pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>8</mn>
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 8\pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 8\pi }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e207b4ba5dd4d7b853328d40285436602d0dc702" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.494ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.9F.AF.E8.A5.BF.E7.A7.AF.E5.88.86.E5.85.AC.E5.BC.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="柯西积分公式">柯西积分公式</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="编辑章节：柯西积分公式">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Factorial05.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="598" data-file-width="760" decoding="async" height="173" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Factorial05.jpg/220px-Factorial05.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Factorial05.jpg/330px-Factorial05.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Factorial05.jpg/440px-Factorial05.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Factorial05.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>複雜的解析函數可以以一系列的流綫和等電位綫（許多以直角相交的曲綫）視覺化，圖中是伽瑪函數的複數對數。</div></div></div>
<p>在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%8D%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90" title="复分析">复分析</a>中，沿<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%8D%E5%B9%B3%E9%9D%A2" title="复平面">复平面</a><a href="/wiki/%E8%8B%A5%E5%B0%94%E5%BD%93%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="若尔当曲线定理">若尔当曲线</a>的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9B%B4%E9%81%93%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86" title="围道积分">围道积分</a>是研究<a href="/wiki/%E8%A7%A3%E6%9E%90%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="解析函数">解析函数</a>的重要手段之一。简化版的<a href="/wiki/%E6%9F%AF%E8%A5%BF%E7%A9%8D%E5%88%86%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="柯西積分公式">柯西積分公式</a>表明，对任意若尔当曲线<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \gamma }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>γ<!-- γ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \gamma }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\gamma " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a223c880b0ce3da8f64ee33c4f0010beee400b1a" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:1.262ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>内任一点<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z_{0}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>z</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>0</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mstyle>

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \oint _{\gamma }{\frac {dz}{z-z_{0}}}=2\pi i.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>该命题是<a href="/wiki/%E6%9F%AF%E8%A5%BF%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="柯西积分定理">柯西积分定理</a>的直接推论，后者表明上述围道积分在围道的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%90%8C%E4%BC%A6" title="同伦">同伦</a>变换下保持不变，因而沿任一曲线的积分和沿以<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z_{0}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</msub>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="z_0" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9e72d1d86e86355892b39b8eb32b964834e113bf" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.135ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>为圆心的圆周积分的结果相同。更为一般地，该公式对不通过<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z_{0}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>一般形式的柯西積分公式建立了<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%A8%E7%BA%AF%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="全纯函数">全纯函数</a> <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(z)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".CE.93.E5.87.BD.E6.95.B0.E4.B8.8E.E6.96.AF.E7.89.B9.E7.81.B5.E5.85.AC.E5.BC.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Γ函数与斯特灵公式">Γ函数与斯特灵公式</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="编辑章节：Γ函数与斯特灵公式">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hopf_Fibration.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="8816" data-file-width="9920" decoding="async" height="196" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/Hopf_Fibration.png/220px-Hopf_Fibration.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/Hopf_Fibration.png/330px-Hopf_Fibration.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/Hopf_Fibration.png/440px-Hopf_Fibration.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hopf_Fibration.png" title="放大"></a></div>通过<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Villarceaux circles" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="维拉瑞索圆"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BB%B4%E6%8B%89%E7%91%9E%E7%B4%A2%E5%9C%86&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="维拉瑞索圆（页面不存在）">维拉瑞索圆</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Villarceaux_circles" title="en:Villarceaux circles"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Villarceaux circles</span></a></span>）</span></span>将三个球面<a href="/wiki/%E9%9C%8D%E6%99%AE%E5%A4%AB%E7%BA%A4%E7%BB%B4%E5%8C%96" title="霍普夫纤维化">霍普夫纤维化</a>，下方是 <a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%8C%E6%AF%94%E5%B0%BC%E2%80%93%E6%96%BD%E5%9B%BE%E8%BF%AA%E5%BA%A6%E9%87%8F" title="富比尼–施图迪度量">富比尼–施图迪度量</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E9%BB%8E%E6%9B%BC%E7%90%83%E9%9D%A2" title="黎曼球面">黎曼球面</a> with its <a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%8C%E6%AF%94%E5%B0%BC%E2%80%93%E6%96%BD%E5%9B%BE%E8%BF%AA%E5%BA%A6%E9%87%8F" title="富比尼–施图迪度量">富比尼–施图迪度量</a> (如图所示的三个平行曲面). 恒等式<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml"><i>S</i><sub>3</sub>(1)/<i>S</i><sub>2</sub>(1) = π/2</span></span>可以确定一个数列。</div></div></div>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%98%B6%E4%B9%98" title="阶乘">阶乘</a>函数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n!}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>

<p>其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \gamma }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
