<p>斯特灵近似的几何应用之一是<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Ehrhart's volume conjecture" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="埃尔哈特体积猜想"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9F%83%E5%B0%94%E5%93%88%E7%89%B9%E4%BD%93%E7%A7%AF%E7%8C%9C%E6%83%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="埃尔哈特体积猜想（页面不存在）">埃尔哈特体积猜想</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ehrhart%27s_volume_conjecture" title="en:Ehrhart's volume conjecture"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Ehrhart's volume conjecture</span></a></span>）</span></span>。将<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>

<h3><span id=".E6.95.B0.E8.AE.BA.E4.B8.8E.E9.BB.8E.E6.9B.BC.CE.B6.E5.87.BD.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="数论与黎曼ζ函数">数论与黎曼ζ函数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="编辑章节：数论与黎曼ζ函数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Pr%C3%BCfer.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="901" data-file-width="1255" decoding="async" height="158" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Pr%C3%BCfer.png/220px-Pr%C3%BCfer.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Pr%C3%BCfer.png/330px-Pr%C3%BCfer.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Pr%C3%BCfer.png/440px-Pr%C3%BCfer.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Pr%C3%BCfer.png" title="放大"></a></div>每个质数都有一个关联的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Prüfer group" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="普魯法群"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%99%AE%E9%AD%AF%E6%B3%95%E7%BE%A4&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="普魯法群（页面不存在）">普魯法群</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pr%C3%BCfer_group" title="en:Prüfer group"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Prüfer group</span></a></span>）</span></span>，即圆的算数定域。分析数论中的<a href="/wiki/L%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="L函數">L函數</a>也定域在每个质数<i>p</i>上。</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ModularGroup-FundamentalDomain-01.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="311" data-file-width="619" decoding="async" height="111" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/ModularGroup-FundamentalDomain-01.png/220px-ModularGroup-FundamentalDomain-01.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/ModularGroup-FundamentalDomain-01.png/330px-ModularGroup-FundamentalDomain-01.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/ModularGroup-FundamentalDomain-01.png/440px-ModularGroup-FundamentalDomain-01.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:ModularGroup-FundamentalDomain-01.png" title="放大"></a></div>基于<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Weil conjecture on Tamagawa numbers" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="韦伊猜想"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9F%A6%E4%BC%8A%E7%8C%9C%E6%83%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="韦伊猜想（页面不存在）">韦伊猜想</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Weil_conjecture_on_Tamagawa_numbers" title="en:Weil conjecture on Tamagawa numbers"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Weil conjecture on Tamagawa numbers</span></a></span>）</span></span>的巴塞尔问题的解：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \zeta (2)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>ζ<!-- ζ --></mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \zeta (2)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \zeta (2)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/eff246e5aba5259593186618c576a3b7e14bc3c8" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.067ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span> 的数值是<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="modular group" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="模群"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%A8%A1%E7%BE%A4&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="模群（页面不存在）">模群</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/modular_group" title="en:modular group"><span dir="auto" lang="en">modular group</span></a></span>）</span></span>中一个基本域的<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%9E%E5%8A%A0%E8%8E%B1%E5%8D%8A%E5%B9%B3%E9%9D%A2%E6%A8%A1%E5%9E%8B" title="庞加莱半平面模型">双曲</a>面积的 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 2\pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>2</mn>

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 2\pi }</annotation>
</semantics>

<p><a href="/wiki/%E9%BB%8E%E6%9B%BC%CE%B6%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="黎曼ζ函數">黎曼ζ函数</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \zeta (s)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \zeta (2)={\frac {1}{1^{2}}}+{\frac {1}{2^{2}}}+{\frac {1}{3^{2}}}+\cdots }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>找到这个无穷级数的<a href="/wiki/%E8%A7%A3%E6%9E%90%E8%A7%A3" title="解析解">解析解</a>是数学界著名的“<a href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B4%E5%A1%9E%E5%B0%94%E9%97%AE%E9%A2%98" title="巴塞尔问题">巴塞尔问题</a>”。1735年，<a href="/wiki/%E8%90%8A%E6%98%82%E5%93%88%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E6%AD%90%E6%8B%89" title="萊昂哈德·歐拉">欧拉</a>解决了这个问题，他得到该无穷级数等于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {\pi ^{2}}{6}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<msup>
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mn>6</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {\pi ^{2}}{6}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {\pi ^{2}}{6}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2e0450af1a6ef356bc0061f8089319332fdde755" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:3.225ex; height:5.676ex;"/></span><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Posamentier_78-1"><a href="#cite_note-Posamentier-78">[76]</a></sup>。欧拉的结论可以推导出一个数论中的结果，即两个随机整数<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%B3%AA" title="互質">互质</a>（即无公因数）的概率为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {6}{\pi ^{2}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {6}{\pi ^{2}}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\frac{6}{\pi^2}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/13b223c2529c136a831d39cc84bd43982bc1abd8" style="vertical-align: -2.171ex; width:3.225ex; height:5.509ex;"/></span> <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-73"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:41–43</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-122"><a href="#cite_note-122">[120]</a></sup>。由于任意整数可由质数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>1</mn>
<msup>
<mi>p</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {1}{p^{2}}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {1}{p^{2}}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/11c4d69a251a144c14c0f73aef3cbaf98462151e" style="vertical-align: -2.505ex; width:3.06ex; height:5.843ex;"/></span>（例如，在所有正整数中，连续7个数中有且只有一个可以被7整除）。因此，任取两个随机整数都能以质数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p}</annotation>
</semantics>

<p>这个结论可以结合<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9A%8F%E6%9C%BA%E6%95%B0%E7%94%9F%E6%88%90%E5%99%A8" title="随机数生成器">随机数生成器</a>，利用<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%92%99%E7%89%B9%E5%8D%A1%E7%BD%97%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95" title="蒙特卡罗方法">蒙特卡罗方法</a>计算<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的近似值。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-74"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:43</sup>
</p><p>﻿巴塞尔问题的结论意味着几何导出量<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的数值与质数的分布有着深刻的关联。巴塞尔问题是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B0%B7%E5%B1%B1%EF%BC%8D%E5%BF%97%E6%9D%91%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="谷山－志村定理">谷山－志村定理</a>的一个特殊情况，是<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Weil's conjecture on Tamagawa numbers" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="安德烈·韦伊对玉河数的猜想"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%89%E5%BE%B7%E7%83%88%C2%B7%E9%9F%A6%E4%BC%8A%E5%AF%B9%E7%8E%89%E6%B2%B3%E6%95%B0%E7%9A%84%E7%8C%9C%E6%83%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="安德烈·韦伊对玉河数的猜想（页面不存在）">安德烈·韦伊对玉河数的猜想</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Weil%27s_conjecture_on_Tamagawa_numbers" title="en:Weil's conjecture on Tamagawa numbers"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Weil's conjecture on Tamagawa numbers</span></a></span>）</span></span>的一个特例，即猜想一个这种形式的算术量关于所有质数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>p</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="p" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81eac1e205430d1f40810df36a0edffdc367af36" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:1.259ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>的无穷乘积能够等于一个几何量——某个<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="locally symmetric space" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="局部对称空间"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B1%80%E9%83%A8%E5%AF%B9%E7%A7%B0%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="局部对称空间（页面不存在）">局部对称空间</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/locally_symmetric_space" title="en:locally symmetric space"><span dir="auto" lang="en">locally symmetric space</span></a></span>）</span></span>体积的倒易。在巴塞尔问题中，这个空间是一个<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="hyperbolic 3-manifold" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="双曲3-流形"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8F%8C%E6%9B%B23-%E6%B5%81%E5%BD%A2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="双曲3-流形（页面不存在）">双曲3-流形</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/hyperbolic_3-manifold" title="en:hyperbolic 3-manifold"><span dir="auto" lang="en">hyperbolic 3-manifold</span></a></span>）</span></span> <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r58896141" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml"><a href="/wiki/SL%E2%82%82(%E2%84%9D)" title="SL₂(ℝ)">SL<sub>2</sub>(<b>R</b>)</a>/<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="modular group" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="模群"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%A8%A1%E7%BE%A4&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="模群（页面不存在）">SL<sub>2</sub>(<b>Z</b>)</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" </p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \zeta }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>除此之外，

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \exp(-\zeta '(0))={\sqrt {2\pi }}.}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \exp(-\zeta '(0))={\sqrt {2\pi }}.}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d2907a3d1a8927b4fd2a276f0463569cc1f77b6f" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:20.12ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>最终的结果是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>可以从<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B0%90%E6%8C%AF%E5%AD%90" title="谐振子">谐振子</a><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="functional determinant" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="泛函行列式"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B3%9B%E5%87%BD%E8%A1%8C%E5%88%97%E5%BC%8F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="泛函行列式（页面不存在）">泛函行列式</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/functional_determinant" title="en:functional determinant"><span dir="auto" lang="en">functional determinant</span></a></span>）</span></span>中求得。这个泛函行列式可以通过一个无穷乘积展开式计算, 而且这种方法等价于<a href="/wiki/%E6%B2%83%E5%88%A9%E6%96%AF%E4%B9%98%E7%A7%AF" title="沃利斯乘积">沃利斯乘积</a>公式。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-125"><a href="#cite_note-125">[123]</a></sup>这种方法可以应用于<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%8F%E5%AD%90%E5%8A%9B%E5%AD%A6" title="量子力学">量子力学</a>, 尤其是<a href="/wiki/%E7%8E%BB%E5%B0%94%E6%A8%A1%E5%9E%8B" title="玻尔模型">玻尔模型</a>中的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%98%E5%88%86%E6%B3%95" title="变分法">变分</a>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-126"><a href="#cite_note-126">[124]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.82.85.E9.87.8C.E5.8F.B6.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="傅里叶级数">傅里叶级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="编辑章节：傅里叶级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:2-adic_integers_with_dual_colorings.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="600" decoding="async" height="220" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/2-adic_integers_with_dual_colorings.svg/220px-2-adic_integers_with_dual_colorings.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/2-adic_integers_with_dual_colorings.svg/330px-2-adic_integers_with_dual_colorings.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/2-adic_integers_with_dual_colorings.svg/440px-2-adic_integers_with_dual_colorings.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:2-adic_integers_with_dual_colorings.svg" title="放大"></a></div><span class="texhtml">π</span>出现在<a href="/wiki/P%E9%80%B2%E6%95%B8" title="P進數">P进数</a>中的表示（如图），它們是<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Prüfer group" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="普魯法群"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%99%AE%E9%AD%AF%E6%B3%95%E7%BE%A4&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="普魯法群（页面不存在）">普魯法群</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pr%C3%BCfer_group" title="en:Prüfer group"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Prüfer group</span></a></span>）</span></span>的元素。<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Tate's thesis" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="泰特的論文"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B3%B0%E7%89%B9%E7%9A%84%E8%AB%96%E6%96%87&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="泰特的論文（页面不存在）">泰特的論文</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tate%27s_thesis" title="en:Tate's thesis"><span dir="auto" <p><a href="/wiki/%E5%91%A8%E6%9C%9F%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="周期函数">周期函数</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E5%82%85%E9%87%8C%E5%8F%B6%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="傅里叶级数">傅里叶级数</a>中，很自然地出现了<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.A8.A1.E5.BD.A2.E5.BC.8F.E4.B8.8E.F0.9D.9C.83.E5.87.BD.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="模形式与𝜃函数">模形式与𝜃函数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="编辑章节：模形式与𝜃函数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>常數<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>與<a href="/wiki/%E6%A8%A1%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F" title="模形式">模形式</a>和<a href="/wiki/%CE%98%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="Θ函數">Θ函數</a>密切相关——比如，<a href="/wiki/%E6%A4%AD%E5%9C%86%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF" title="椭圆曲线">椭圆曲线</a>中的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="j-invariant" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="j变量"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=J%E5%8F%98%E9%87%8F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="J变量（页面不存在）">j变量</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/j-invariant" title="en:j-invariant"><span dir="auto" lang="en">j-invariant</span></a></span>）</span></span>就很大程度上涉及到了<a href="/wiki/%E6%A5%9A%E5%BE%B7%E8%AF%BA%E5%A4%AB%E6%96%AF%E5%9F%BA%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95" title="楚德诺夫斯基算法">楚德诺夫斯基算法</a>（一种快速计算<span class="texhtml">π</span>的方法）。
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E6%A8%A1%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F" title="模形式">模形式</a>是以在<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%8A%E5%8D%8A%E5%B9%B3%E9%9D%A2" title="上半平面">上半平面</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%A8%E7%BA%AF%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="全纯函数">全純函數</a>的在<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="modular group" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="模群"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%A8%A1%E7%BE%A4&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="模群（页面不存在）">模群</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/modular_group" title="en:modular group"><span dir="auto" lang="en">modular group</span></a></span>）</span></span><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle SL_{2}(\mathbb {Z} )}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>它是一種名為<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Jacobi form" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="雅可比形式"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%85%E5%8F%AF%E6%AF%94%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="雅可比形式（页面不存在）">雅可比形式</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jacobi_form" title="en:Jacobi form"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Jacobi form</span></a></span>）</span></span>的模形式，<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Mumford_1983_1–117_129-0"><a href="#cite_note-Mumford_1983_1–117-129">[127]</a></sup>有時以<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="nome (mathematics)" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="諾姆 (數學)"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%AB%BE%E5%A7%86_(%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="諾姆 (數學)（页面不存在）">諾姆</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nome_(mathematics)" title="en:nome (mathematics)"><span dir="auto" lang="en">nome (mathematics)</span></a></span>）</span></span><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle q=e^{\pi i\tau }}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>常數<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是一個特殊的常數，它會使雅可比<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \Theta }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \Theta }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\Theta" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bc927b19f46d005b4720db7a0f96cd5b6f1a0d9b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.808ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>函數形成<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E5%AE%88%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F" title="自守形式">自守形式</a>，即該函數會以特定方式變換。有若干恆等式在所有自守形式下成立。，例如：
</p>

<p>它使得<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \theta }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.9F.AF.E8.A5.BF.E5.88.86.E5.B8.83.E4.B8.8E.E4.BD.8D.E5.8A.BF.E8.AE.BA"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="柯西分布与位势论">柯西分布与位势论</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="编辑章节：柯西分布与位势论">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Witch_of_Agnesi,_construction.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="223" data-file-width="398" decoding="async" height="123" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Witch_of_Agnesi%2C_construction.svg/220px-Witch_of_Agnesi%2C_construction.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Witch_of_Agnesi%2C_construction.svg/330px-Witch_of_Agnesi%2C_construction.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Witch_of_Agnesi%2C_construction.svg/440px-Witch_of_Agnesi%2C_construction.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Witch_of_Agnesi,_construction.svg" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E7%AE%95%E8%88%8C%E7%BA%BF" title="箕舌线">箕舌线</a>，其英文名来源于<a href="/wiki/%E7%91%AA%E9%BA%97%E4%BA%9E%C2%B7%E5%8A%A0%E5%9F%83%E5%A1%94%E7%B4%8D%C2%B7%E9%98%BF%E6%B6%85%E8%A5%BF" title="瑪麗亞·加埃塔納·阿涅西">玛利亚·阿涅西</a>（1718–1799），是柯西分布的一个几何构筑图。</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E6%9F%AF%E8%A5%BF%E5%88%86%E5%B8%83" title="柯西分布">柯西分布</a>：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle g(x)={\frac {1}{\pi }}\cdot {\frac {1}{x^{2}+1}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle g(x)={\frac {1}{\pi }}\cdot {\frac {1}{x^{2}+1}}}</annotation>

<p>是一个<a href="/wiki/%E6%A9%9F%E7%8E%87%E5%AF%86%E5%BA%A6%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="機率密度函數">概率密度函数</a>。其总概率等于1，因为下列积分：
</p>

<p>柯西分布的香农熵等于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \log(4\pi )}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:130px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Brownianmotion_beads_in_water_spim_video.gif"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="128" data-file-width="128" decoding="async" height="128" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/5/5a/Brownianmotion_beads_in_water_spim_video.gif" width="128"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Brownianmotion_beads_in_water_spim_video.gif" title="放大"></a></div>柯西分布控制做<a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%83%E6%9C%97%E8%BF%90%E5%8A%A8" title="布朗运动">布朗运动</a>的粒子通过膜的通道</div></div></div>
<p>柯西分布在位势论中扮演着重要的角色因为它是最简单的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Furstenberg boundary" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="福斯坦堡测度"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%A6%8F%E6%96%AF%E5%9D%A6%E5%A0%A1%E6%B5%8B%E5%BA%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="福斯坦堡测度（页面不存在）">福斯坦堡测度</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Furstenberg_boundary" title="en:Furstenberg boundary"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Furstenberg boundary</span></a></span>）</span></span>和与在半平面上做布朗运动相关联的经典泊松核<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-130"><a href="#cite_note-130">[128]</a></sup>。<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Conjugate harmonic function" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="共轭谐波函数"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%85%B1%E8%BD%AD%E8%B0%90%E6%B3%A2%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="共轭谐波函数（页面不存在）">共轭谐波函数</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Conjugate_harmonic_function" title="en:Conjugate harmonic function"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Conjugate harmonic function</span></a></span>）</span></span>以及<a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%8C%E7%88%BE%E4%BC%AF%E7%89%B9%E8%BD%89%E6%8F%9B" title="希爾伯特轉換">希尔伯特变换</a>与泊松核的渐近线有关。 希尔伯特变换<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle H}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle Hf(t)={\frac {1}{\pi }}\int _{-\infty }^{\infty }{\frac {f(x)}{x-t}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>常数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>

</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.A4.87.E8.AE.8A.E5.8B.95.E6.85.8B.E7.B3.BB.E7.B5.B1"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="複變動態系統">複變動態系統</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="编辑章节：複變動態系統">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mandel_zoom_00_mandelbrot_set.jpg"><img alt="一個複數平面下，曼德博集合的黑色圖案，背景為藍色的" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1920" data-file-width="2560" decoding="async" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Mandel_zoom_00_mandelbrot_set.jpg/220px-Mandel_zoom_00_mandelbrot_set.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Mandel_zoom_00_mandelbrot_set.jpg/330px-Mandel_zoom_00_mandelbrot_set.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Mandel_zoom_00_mandelbrot_set.jpg/440px-Mandel_zoom_00_mandelbrot_set.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mandel_zoom_00_mandelbrot_set.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>可以從<a href="/wiki/%E6%9B%BC%E5%BE%B7%E5%8D%9A%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88" title="曼德博集合">曼德博集合</a>中計算<span class="texhtml">π</span>，計算方式和計算從(−0.75, ε)點開始，一直到發散之前的次數有關</div></div></div>
<p>大衛·波爾（David Boll）在1991年發現在<a href="/wiki/%E6%9B%BC%E5%BE%B7%E5%8D%9A%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88" title="曼德博集合">曼德博集合</a><a href="/wiki/%E5%88%86%E5%BD%A2" title="分形">分形</a>中也有<span class="texhtml">π</span>的出現<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-KA_133-0"><a href="#cite_note-KA-133">[131]</a></sup>。他檢查在曼德博集合在<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (-0.75,0)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle (0.25,\varepsilon )}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bcda1b27646c453dc2dba6af6e1d745c6308b585" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:8.061ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>也會有類似的特性：在發散之前迭代的次數和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \varepsilon }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>

</p>
<h2><span id=".E6.95.B0.E5.AD.A6.E4.B9.8B.E5.A4.96.E7.9A.84.CF.80"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="数学之外的π">数学之外的<span class="texhtml">π</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="编辑章节：数学之外的π">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E6.8F.8F.E8.BF.B0.E7.89.A9.E7.90.86.E7.8E.B0.E8.B1.A1"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="描述物理现象">描述物理现象</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="编辑章节：描述物理现象">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>即便<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>不是一个<a href="/wiki/%E7%89%A9%E7%90%86%E5%B8%B8%E6%95%B8" title="物理常數">物理常数</a>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>

<p>海森堡不确定性原理是量子力学的一个基本公式，它表明在对一个粒子测量时，其位置不确定度（<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \Delta x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \Delta x\,\Delta p\geq {\frac {h}{4\pi }}.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle m}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p><a href="/wiki/%E6%B5%81%E9%AB%94%E5%8B%95%E5%8A%9B%E5%AD%B8" title="流體動力學">流體動力學</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%AF%E6%89%98%E5%85%8B%E6%96%AF%E5%AE%9A%E5%BE%8B" title="斯托克斯定律">斯托克斯定律</a>中也有<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>。斯托克斯定律是半径约为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle R}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>R</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle R}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4b0bfb3769bf24d80e15374dc37b0441e2616e33" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的小球體在<a href="/wiki/%E9%BB%8F%E5%BA%A6" title="黏度">黏度</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \eta }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>η<!-- η --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \eta }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\eta " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e4d701857cf5fbec133eebaf94deadf722537f64" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:1.169ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B5%81%E9%AB%94" title="流體">流體</a>中以速度<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle v}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>v</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle v}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="v" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e07b00e7fc0847fbd16391c778d65bc25c452597" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.128ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>運動時會受到的<a href="/wiki/%E9%98%BB%E5%8A%9B" title="阻力">阻力</a>满足<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139"><a href="#cite_note-139">[137]</a></sup>：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle F=6\,\pi \,\eta \,R\,v.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mo>=</mo>
<mn>6</mn>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>η<!-- η --></mi>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>R</mi>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>v</mi>
<mo>.</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle F=6\,\pi \,\eta \,R\,v.}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle F=6\,\pi \,\eta \,R\,v.}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/56fa1c87a5fa2e77f6f0705a882182b2a41d846e" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:13.59ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>在理想状态下，一个河流的曲折程度——也就是河道本身的长度与源头到入海口的比值——随着时间的推移逐渐趋向于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>。河流外边缘的快速水流的弯曲会导致河流内边缘加倍的侵蚀，而河道因此变得更加弯曲，使得整个河流弯折得更加厉害。然而，这股弯折劲儿最终会导致河流折回一开始弯折的地方，导致“短路”，并在此过程中形成一个<a href="/wiki/%E6%B2%B3%E8%BF%B9%E6%B9%96" title="河迹湖">河迹湖</a>。这两种相反的因素使得河道长度与源头到入海口的比值的平均值为<span class="texhtml">π</span>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140"><a href="#cite_note-140">[138]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141"><a href="#cite_note-141">[139]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id=".CF.80.E7.9A.84.E8.AE.B0.E5.BF.86.E6.8A.80.E5.B7.A7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="π的记忆技巧"><span class="texhtml">π</span>的记忆技巧</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="编辑章节：π的记忆技巧">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%CE%A0%E6%96%87%E5%AD%97%E5%AD%B8" title="Π文字學">π文字学</a></div>
<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%CE%A0%E6%96%87%E5%AD%97%E5%AD%B8" title="Π文字學">π文字學</a>（或譯作圆周率<span class="texhtml">π</span>的语言学）是指人们記住<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>大量的位值<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-75"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:44–45</sup>，并将其世界紀錄載於<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%81%A5%E5%8A%9B%E5%A3%AB%E4%B8%96%E7%95%8C%E7%B4%80%E9%8C%84%E5%A4%A7%E5%85%A8" title="健力士世界紀錄大全">健力士世界紀錄大全</a>中的做法。維爾·米納（Rajveer Meena）於2015年3月21日在印度於9小時27分鐘內背誦了7萬位的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>，创下健力士世界紀錄大全認證的世界紀錄。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142"><a href="#cite_note-142">[140]</a></sup>2006年，日本退休工程師<a href="/wiki/%E5%8E%9F%E5%8F%A3%E8%AD%89" title="原口證">原口證</a>，自稱已經背誦了十萬個小數位，但他未獲健力士世界紀錄大全認證。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-japantimes_143-0"><a href="#cite_note-japantimes-143">[141]</a></sup>
</p><p>一個常用於記憶<span class="texhtml">π</span>的技巧是背誦一個以單詞的長度代表<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>數值的故事或詩歌：第一個單詞有三個字母，第二個單詞有一個字母，第三個單詞有四個字母，第四個單詞有一個字母，第五個單詞有五個字母，如此類推。一個早期的例子是由英國科學家<a href="/wiki/%E8%A9%B9%E5%A7%86%E5%A3%AB%C2%B7%E9%87%91%E6%96%AF" title="詹姆士·金斯">詹姆士·金斯</a>設計的詩歌：「<span lang="en">How I want a drink, alcoholic of course, after the heavy lectures involving quantum mechanics.</span>」<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-76"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:44–45</sup>這一類的詩歌有時在英文中稱為「<span lang="en">piem</span>」。除了英文，用於記憶<span class="texhtml">π</span>的詩歌亦有不同語言的版本<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-77"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:44-45</sup>。但是，創下紀錄的記憶<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的人一般並不以詩歌記憶<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>，而是用如記憶數字規律或<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="method of loci" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="軌跡法"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%BB%8C%E8%B7%A1%E6%B3%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="軌跡法（页面不存在）">軌跡法</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/method_of_loci" title="en:method of loci"><span dir="auto" lang="en">method of loci</span></a></span>）</span></span>的方法。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-144"><a href="#cite_note-144">[142]</a></sup>
</p><p>有好幾位作家仿照上述记忆技巧，用<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的數值創作了新型的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="constrained writing" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="約束寫作"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%B4%84%E6%9D%9F%E5%AF%AB%E4%BD%9C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="約束寫作（页面不存在）">約束寫作</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/constrained_writing" title="en:constrained writing"><span dir="auto" lang="en">constrained writing</span></a></span>）</span></span>方式，其中單詞的長度須符合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的數值。《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Cadaeic Cadenza" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="The Cadaeic Cadenza"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=The_Cadaeic_Cadenza&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="The Cadaeic Cadenza（页面不存在）">The Cadaeic Cadenza</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cadaeic_Cadenza" title="en:Cadaeic Cadenza"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Cadaeic Cadenza</span></a></span>）</span></span>》以上述技巧包含了<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>前3835位的值<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-145"><a href="#cite_note-145">[143]</a></sup>，一本標準長度的書《Not a Wake》有一萬個單詞，其中每個單詞亦代表了<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的一個位值。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-KeithNAW_146-0"><a href="#cite_note-KeithNAW-146">[144]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.A4.A7.E4.BC.97.E6.96.87.E5.8C.96.E4.B8.AD.E7.9A.84.CF.80"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="大众文化中的π">大众文化中的<span class="texhtml">π</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="编辑章节：大众文化中的π">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Pi_pie2.jpg"><img alt="Pi Pie at Delft University" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="576" data-file-width="577" decoding="async" height="220" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Pi_pie2.jpg/220px-Pi_pie2.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Pi_pie2.jpg/330px-Pi_pie2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Pi_pie2.jpg/440px-Pi_pie2.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Pi_pie2.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>一個<span class="texhtml">π</span>派。圓形的<a href="/wiki/%E8%A5%BF%E5%BC%8F%E9%A4%A1%E9%A4%85" title="西式餡餅">西式餡餅</a>是個常見的<span class="texhtml">π</span><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9B%99%E9%97%9C%E8%AA%9E" title="雙關語">雙關語</a>（在英語中，圓周率和派的發音相同）。</div></div></div>
<p>也許因為<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的公式很簡短而且四處可見， <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>比其他數學常数在流行文化中更常見<span id="noteTag-cite_ref-sup"><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149"><a href="#cite_note-149">[註 3]</a></sup></span>。
</p><p>在2008年由<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8B%B1%E5%9C%8B%E5%85%AC%E9%96%8B%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%B8" title="英國公開大學">英國公開大學</a>及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8B%B1%E5%9C%8B%E5%BB%A3%E6%92%AD%E5%85%AC%E5%8F%B8" title="英國廣播公司">英國廣播公司</a>聯合制作的記錄片《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="The Story of Maths" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="数学的故事"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%95%85%E4%BA%8B&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="数学的故事（页面不存在）">数学的故事</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Story_of_Maths" title="en:The Story of Maths"><span dir="auto" lang="en">The Story of Maths</span></a></span>）</span></span>》于2008年十月由<a href="/wiki/%E8%8B%B1%E5%9C%8B%E5%BB%A3%E6%92%AD%E5%85%AC%E5%8F%B8%E7%AC%AC%E5%9B%9B%E5%8F%B0" title="英國廣播公司第四台">英國廣播公司第四台</a>播放。影片讲述了英國數學家<a href="/wiki/%E9%A9%AC%E5%BA%93%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E6%9D%9C%C2%B7%E7%B4%A2%E6%89%98%E4%BC%8A" title="马库斯·杜·索托伊">马库斯·杜·索托伊</a>在到訪印度研究當地三角學的貢獻時，展示出歷史上<span class="texhtml">π</span>最精確的計算公式的<a href="/wiki/%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%E5%9B%BE%E5%BD%A2" title="信息图形">信息图形</a> 。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBC_2008_150-0"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_2008-150">[147]</a></sup>
</p><p>在巴黎的科学博物馆<a href="/wiki/%E7%99%BC%E7%8F%BE%E5%AE%AE" title="發現宮">發現宮</a>中有一個稱為「<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>房」的圓形房間。牆上刻有<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的707位數字。數字貼在圓頂狀的天花板上，由大型的木製字符組成。數值是1853年由英國數學家<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="William Shanks" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="威廉·尚克思"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A8%81%E5%BB%89%C2%B7%E5%B0%9A%E5%85%8B%E6%80%9D&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="威廉·尚克思（页面不存在）">威廉·尚克思</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shanks" title="en:William Shanks"><span dir="auto" lang="en">William Shanks</span></a></span>）</span></span>的計算結果，但是该结果於第528位后開始出現謬誤，其在1946年發現，1949年修正。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151"><a href="#cite_note-151">[148]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-78"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:50</sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%A1%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E8%90%A8%E6%A0%B9" title="卡尔·萨根">卡尔·萨根</a>的小说《<a href="/wiki/%E6%8E%A5%E8%A7%B8%E6%9C%AA%E4%BE%86_(%E5%B0%8F%E8%AA%AA)" title="接觸未來 (小說)">接觸未來</a>》中则暗示说，宇宙的创造者在<span class="texhtml">π</span>的数字中暗藏了一则信息。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152"><a href="#cite_note-152">[149]</a></sup><span class="texhtml">π</span>的数字也用在<a href="/wiki/%E5%87%B1%E7%89%B9%C2%B7%E5%B8%83%E5%B8%8C" title="凱特·布希">凱特·布希</a>所出的专辑<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Aerial (album)" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="Aerial (album)"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Aerial_(album)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Aerial (album)（页面不存在）">Aerial</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aerial_(album)" title="en:Aerial (album)"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Aerial (album)</span></a></span>）</span></span>中的《Pi》的歌词里。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153"><a href="#cite_note-153">[150]</a></sup>
</p><p>在美国，人们在3月14日庆祝<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87%E6%97%A5" title="圓周率日">圓周率日</a>，一个在学生中很流行的节日。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154"><a href="#cite_note-154">[151]</a></sup>一些自称“数学<a href="/wiki/%E6%9E%81%E5%AE%A2" title="极客">极客</a>”的人常常用<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\tau " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/38a7dcde9730ef0853809fefc18d88771f95206c" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.202ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的使用还并没有在数学界成为主流。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163"><a href="#cite_note-163">[160]</a></sup>
</p><p>在1897年，一个业余的美国数学家试图通过<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%B0%E7%AC%AC%E5%AE%89%E7%BA%B3%E5%B7%9E%E8%AE%AE%E4%BC%9A" title="印第安纳州议会">印第安纳州议会</a>来通过後世所謂<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%B0%E7%AC%AC%E5%AE%89%E7%BA%B3%E5%9C%86%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87%E6%B3%95%E6%A1%88" title="印第安纳圆周率法案">印第安纳圆周率法案</a>的法案。这一法案因试图以法律命令强制规定一个数学常数而臭名远扬。该法案描述了一个<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8C%96%E5%9C%86%E4%B8%BA%E6%96%B9" title="化圆为方">化圆为方</a>的方法，并间接提到了<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的错误值，例如3.2。该法案通过了印第安纳州众议院的表决，但是被参议院否决。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Arndt_2-79"><a href="#cite_note-Arndt-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:211–212</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164"><a href="#cite_note-164">[161]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-165"><a href="#cite_note-165">[162]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id=".E6.B3.A8.E9.87.8A"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="注释">注释</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="编辑章节：注释">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div id="references-NoteFoot"><ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-27"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-27">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">这个<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%9A%E9%A1%B9%E5%BC%8F" title="多项式">多项式</a>是<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E5%BC%A6" title="正弦">正弦</a>函数的<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%B0%E5%8B%92%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="泰勒级数">泰勒级数</a>展开的前三项。</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-53"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-53">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">依照<a href="/wiki/%E8%83%A1%E5%A4%AB%E9%87%91%E5%AD%97%E5%A1%94" title="胡夫金字塔">胡夫金字塔</a>，那些和金字塔高度一致的圆形，周长应等同于金字塔底部的周长（即高度为280<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%98_(%E5%96%AE%E4%BD%8D)" title="肘 (單位)">肘</a>，周长为1760<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%98_(%E5%96%AE%E4%BD%8D)" title="肘 (單位)">肘</a>）<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52"><a href="#cite_note-52">[51]</a></sup>。</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-149"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-149">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">例如，柯利弗德·皮寇弗稱<span class="texhtml">π</span>為「最知名的數學常数」，皮特森則寫道：「在所有數學常數當中，<span class="texhtml">π</span>一向最受瞩目。」例如<a href="/wiki/%E7%B4%80%E6%A2%B5%E5%B8%8C" title="紀梵希">紀梵希</a><span class="texhtml">π</span>香水、<a href="/wiki/%CE%A0_(%E9%9B%BB%E5%BD%B1)" title="Π (電影)">Π (電影)</a>以及<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87%E6%97%A5" title="圓周率日">圓周率日</a>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147"><a href="#cite_note-147">[145]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148"><a href="#cite_note-148">[146]</a></sup></span>
</li>
</ol></div>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.83.E8.80.83.E8.B3.87.E6.96.99"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="參考資料">參考資料</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="编辑章节：參考資料">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

</div><p>．2014 houkouonchi found pi to  28472 Decimal places

<li id="cite_note-12"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-12">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation journal">Boeing, Niels. <a class="external text" href="http://www.zeit.de/zeit-wissen/2016/02/pi-tag-mathematik-pi-kreiszahl" rel="nofollow">存档副本 <bdi lang="de">Die Welt ist Pi</bdi> [The World is Pi]</a>. Zeit Online. 2016-03-14 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2016-09-13</span>]</span>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20160317050313/http://www.zeit.de/zeit-wissen/2016/02/pi-tag-mathematik-pi-kreiszahl" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2016-03-17） <span style="font-family: sans-serif; cursor: default; color:#555; font-size: 0.8em; bottom: 0.1em; font-weight: bold;" title="连接到德语网页">（德语）</span>. <q><span lang="de">Die Ludolphsche Zahl oder Kreiszahl erhielt nun auch das Symbol, unter dem wir es heute kennen: William Jones schlug 1706 den griechischen Buchstaben π vor, in Anlehnung an perimetros, griechisch für Umfang. Leonhard Euler etablierte π schließlich in seinen mathematischen Schriften.</span>中文：“鲁道夫数”，或称“圆周率”，同样獲得一个如今广为人知的符号——威廉·琼斯1706年提出使用字母<span class="texhtml">π</span>，因为这是希腊语“周长”（περίμετρος）的开头字母。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8E%B1%E6%98%82%E5%93%88%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89" title="莱昂哈德·欧拉">莱昂哈德·欧拉</a>在其数学著作中確立了<span class="texhtml">π</span>的使用。</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87&amp;rft.atitle=%E5%AD%98%E6%A1%A3%E5%89%AF%E6%9C%AC+Die+Welt+ist+Pi&amp;rft.aufirst=Niels&amp;rft.aulast=Boeing&amp;rft.date=2016-03-14&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=Zeit+Online&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.zeit.de%2Fzeit-wissen%2F2016%2F02%2Fpi-tag-mathematik-pi-kreiszahl&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> are sufficient to calculate the volume of the universe to the nearest atom.”（中文：39位<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>已经足以计算宇宙到其最近的原子的体积了。）<br/>鉴于人们需要一些额外的数位来解决捨入誤差的问题，阿恩特称几百位小数足以应付任何科学计算了。</span>

<li><a class="external text" href="http://www16.big.or.jp/~bunnywk/superpi.html" rel="nofollow">SuperPI</a>（<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20160907224458/http://www16.big.or.jp/~bunnywk/superpi.html" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>） 計算π值的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%BB%9F%E9%AB%94" title="軟體">軟體</a>，電腦<a class="mw-redirect mw-disambig" href="/wiki/%E7%A1%AC%E9%AB%94" title="硬體">硬體</a>玩家常用來測試<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E8%85%A6" title="電腦">電腦</a>運算速度（日文）</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20080123152938/http://www.jason314.com/" rel="nofollow">計算圓周率</a></li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://numbers.computation.free.fr/Constants/PiProgram/pifast.html" rel="nofollow">PiFast</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20071013210256/http://numbers.computation.free.fr/Constants/PiProgram/pifast.html" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>） 個人電腦上最快的計算π值軟體，是個人電腦計算π值紀錄保持軟體。</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://dovsherman.deviantart.com/art/Calculating-Pi-with-a-Cannon-25649357" rel="nofollow">用大炮求圓周率</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20160218101825/http://dovsherman.deviantart.com/art/Calculating-Pi-with-a-Cannon-25649357" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）：以<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%92%99%E7%89%B9%E5%8D%A1%E7%BD%97%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95" title="蒙特卡罗算法">蒙特卡羅演算法</a>，利用<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86%E7%9A%84%E9%9D%A2%E7%A7%AF" title="圆的面积">圓的面積</a>求圓周率。</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="http://www.geom.uiuc.edu/~huberty/math5337/groupe/digits.html" rel="nofollow">展示将π值计算到10万位的一个网站</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20201127175450/http://www.geom.uiuc.edu/~huberty/math5337/groupe/digits.html" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）</li></ul>
